  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_949f0976-fee9-415d-931a-04b72b8560c8'
      });
    }

    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548171597?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548171597" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer11969978315647559122"><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411465i/808252._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><img width='100%' src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411465i/808253._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>4.5 stars<br/><br/><b> A dark, emotional read filled with pain and loss but also love and hope. It reminds you how precious life is and how, even in the darkest of times, hope can always shine though. </b><br/><br/>You know how sometimes you come across a book where you read the blurb and it just makes you want to drop everything in your life so you can read it? This book did that to me. From the moment I heard about it, I couldn’t stop thinking about it.<br/><br/>The dedication set the tone for the story. Heavy. Emotional. Hitting</span>
  <span id="freeText11969978315647559122" style="display:none"><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411465i/808252._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411465i/808253._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>4.5 stars<br><br><b> A dark, emotional read filled with pain and loss but also love and hope. It reminds you how precious life is and how, even in the darkest of times, hope can always shine though. </b><br><br>You know how sometimes you come across a book where you read the blurb and it just makes you want to drop everything in your life so you can read it? This book did that to me. From the moment I heard about it, I couldn’t stop thinking about it.<br><br>The dedication set the tone for the story. Heavy. Emotional. Hitting you right in the heart.<br><br><i> <b> “This book is for anyone who has ever lost a loved one, for anyone who has woken up crying and gone to bed the same way, for anyone who has had to learn that it’s okay to not be okay. Surviving isn’t strength, it’s continuing to breathe one day at a time; strength is learning to live despite the pain.” </b></i> <br><br>I love Jasinda Wilder’s writing. She made me fall in love. She ripped out my heart. She made me grieve. But then she made me move on. Not forget, but just move forward. And find a way to be happy again. I truly felt like I went through the journey with the heroine.<br><br>Kyle and Nell grew up together. They’d been inseparable since they were babies and it was almost inevitable that they end up together. Everyone almost expected it and for so many reasons, they were just perfect for each other.<br><br>The author captured both the thrill and fumbling perfection of first love – the awkwardness, curiosity, desire, hope… I felt it all. But at the same time, I read with a certain sense of dread. Because of the blurb and the teaser chapter, I knew what was coming and I dreaded it.<br><br>But regardless of knowing it was coming, “that” scene still ripped my heart out again and made my cry. I felt it so strongly. Felt it to my core.<br><br>After Kyle’s death (not a spoiler, because it’s mentioned in the blurb), I just read scene after scene constantly on the verge of tears. When Nell cried, I cried with her. I could feel how broken she was with all my heart. And it was just shattering.<br><br><i> “I wanted nothing more than to climb into the box with him and quit breathing, find him in whatever came after life.” </i> <br><br>At the funeral was where Nell saw Colton for the first time since she was a kid. He was the complete opposite of Kyle. The bad boy to Kyle’s golden boy reputation. Rugged, tattooed, and most importantly, understanding of her pain. He offered her comfort without question or judgment.<br><br><i> <b> “I hold her. I don’t tell her it’s okay.<br>“Be mad,” I say. “Be hurt. Be broken. Cry.” </b></i>  <br><br>They just had this… connection. It was subtle and unspoken. But, without a doubt, there.<br><br>At first, there was the tiniest feeling of ‘too soon’ for me. But the more I think about it now, the more I understand it. She loved Kyle because it made sense. He was her best friend and everything in life had pointed them right at each other. But what she felt for Colton was never predestined, it just was. Undeniably so.<br><br>At this point we are treated to Colton’s POV. Two years later, in NYC, Colton runs into Nell and can see that she has still not let go of the pain of losing Kyle. It still haunts her and he is determined to help her through it.<br><br><i> “I can’t fix her. I know this too. I’m not going to try. I’ve had too many goody-goody girls hook up with me, thinking they can fix me. I also know I’m not going to stay away.” </i><br><br>Colton understood her. Deeply. Having suffered through a very different childhood than his brother, he understands pain. He’s not trying to get her to move on, but just to allow herself to feel the pain. To let it in and to deal with it.<br><br><i> <b> “We understand each other, Nelly. We’ve both lost someone we love. We both have scars and regrets and anger. We can do this together.”<br><br>“I can’t be fixed.”<br>“You’re committed to being broken forever?”<br>“Goddamit, Colton. Why are you doing this? You don’t know me.”<br>“I want to.” It’s the answer to both of her statements. </b></i>  <br><br>This book deals with some heavy themes and the story was emotional but there were also several moments that had me snorting with laughter.<br><br>Music played a big part in this book as well. It gave a voice to the pain. A voice to the emotions that were bottled up deep inside. The songs really got to me and I cried while reading almost every one.<br><br>There were both 5 star moments in this book as well as a few that made me go squinty-eyed but over all, I loved the story.<br><br>The novel is a great length – not too long, not too short. It gives you plenty of time to connect with the characters. It’ll rip out your heart, but it’ll also allow you to heal and leave you in a happy place.<br><br>If you are looking for a new, emotional read, this would be a great choice.<br><br><i> <b> “… when you feel that kind of all-consuming need for someone, a person you’d do fucking anything for, no matter what? They’re in your fucking skin, in your soul, like the essence of who they are is imprinted on you so completely like the very air you breathe… That’s love.” </b></i> <br><br>Here's my casting:<br><br>Colton:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411465i/808254._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Nell:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411465i/808255.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Kyle:<br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411465i/808256.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img width="100%" src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411465i/808257._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b> TEASER CHAPTER AVAILABLE HERE: </b><br><a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.jasindawilder.com/2013/03/08/falling-into-you-full-chapter-and-cover-tease/">http://www.jasindawilder.com/2013/03/...</a><br><br><i> I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first. Kyle was my first one true love, my first in every way.<br><br>Then, one stormy August night, he died, and the person I was died with him.<br><br>Colton didn't teach me how to live. He didn't heal the pain. He didn't make it okay. He taught me how to hurt, how to not be okay, and, eventually, how to let go.<br><br><b> For more of my reviews, visit <a href="http://aestasbookblog.com" rel="nofollow noopener">Aestas Book Blog</a><br><br>And come join the Aestas Book Blog <a href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Aestas-Book-Blog/332404836826905" rel="nofollow noopener"> Facebook Page</a><br><br></b></i> Thank you Jasinda Wilder for providing me an ARC to review.</span>
  <a data-text-id="11969978315647559122" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_560220319" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/560220319" />
    <a title="~ Becs ~" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2626261-becs"><img alt="~ Becs ~" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1388693144p2/2626261.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/560220319?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="~ Becs ~" class="user" itemprop="url" name="~ Becs ~" href="/user/show/2626261-becs">~ Becs ~</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=made-me-cry">made-me-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tattooed-hero">tattooed-hero</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=cover-lust-i-has-it">cover-lust-i-has-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=tragic">tragic</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2626261-becs?shelf=smuttastic">smuttastic</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer560220319" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10904048706988632327"><b>
  <blockquote>Oh. Mon. Dieu!!</blockquote>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413258i/813438.jpg' alt=' photo coltquote_zps3529e475.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>This was such a rollercoaster of a book as you run the gamut of so many emotions. It takes you from sappy happy right down to the depths of despair and then guides you slowly back to happiness but not without an deeply anguished journey first.<br/><br/>I guess, if you’re reading my review, then you’ve read the blurb above. As you read the first part of the novel about Nell and Kyle and their budding high school romance you know that something terrible is just around the corner and, as y</span>
  <span id="freeText10904048706988632327" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>Oh. Mon. Dieu!!</blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413258i/813438.jpg" alt=" photo coltquote_zps3529e475.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>This was such a rollercoaster of a book as you run the gamut of so many emotions. It takes you from sappy happy right down to the depths of despair and then guides you slowly back to happiness but not without an deeply anguished journey first.<br><br>I guess, if you’re reading my review, then you’ve read the blurb above. As you read the first part of the novel about Nell and Kyle and their budding high school romance you know that something terrible is just around the corner and, as you read it, you can feel the sorrow coming. It’s a beautiful part of the story, high school friends slowly becoming boyfriend and girlfriend and, eventually, becoming lovers. It’s beautifully done but it’s tinged with incredible sadness as you know that it’s about to be ripped away from them. And, when it did, it was so awful, so very tragic that I cried right along with Nell.<br><br>At Kyle’s funeral Nell is trying to lock away her grief, to not give it an outlet and Colt, Kyle’s older brother sees this – they spend a bit of time together. There’s an electric connection between them but both of them realise how inappropriate this is at this time and they ignore it. We jump forward two years when Nell and Colt are both now living in New York and they bump into one another again.<br><br>As we catch up with Nell, two years after the tragedy that took Kyle from her, it’s apparent that she is hurting badly. She’s in so much emotional pain, so many shards and jags in her soul and she’s cutting herself to make her forget the pain, to feel another kind of pain. She’s carrying a huge amount of survivor’s guilt and feels completely responsible for Kyle’s death, for being alive and in the world when he isn’t. She’s never let that grief out and now it’s eating away at her like a cancer, changing who she is, not allowing her to get on with her life. She’s just a guilt-ravaged shell of the carefree, optimistic, hopeful girl she once was.<br><br>Colton has also had his share of tragedy and a difficult past and he completely recognises the pain that he sees in Nell. That zinging connection they shared two years ago has never gone away and they cannot resist for long and they literally fall into one another, healing each other. The sex between these two is seriously off the charts HOT and I would advise against reading it in your lunch break at work and then expecting to concentrate for the afternoon. My Bad!!<br><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>You bite your lip, and I want to take that lip into my mouth and suck on it like a popsicle. I want to lick your lips and bite them and kiss you until you’re fucking lost and gasping and puddled on the floor.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><br><b>Holy Fuck!!</b><br><br><br>Jasinda Wilder is, I think, such a talented writer. She takes the issue of self-harm and handles it so sensitively. So many people who harm themselves are doing this to block out another kind of pain – often abuse, chronic medical conditions, deep emotional pain. This is the case of Nell – she hurts herself to block out the all-consuming guilt and grief she harbours over Kyle’s death. I thought this was incredibly well done.<br><br>Colt understands her and why she does it – he doesn’t like it and is determined that she won’t do it again. He’s had a difficult life so far, has done many things he regrets and all that emotional pain walled up inside Nell is deeply familiar to him. It’s beautiful to watch how they slowly shared their experiences with one another and gave all that awful grief an outlet. They heal one another.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>We understand each other, Nelly. We’ve both lost someone we love. We both have scars and regrets and anger. We can do this together.</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Despite all this, there is humour to be found – it’s not all an angst-ridden story and they often made me laugh.<br><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“Oh god…” I whimper. <br>“I haven’t done anything yet baby,” Colton growls. <br>“I know,” I pant. “I was just saying your name.”</blockquote>
</b><br><br> <br>Jasinda Wilder made me cry, she made me happy, she even made me laugh but most of all she gave me a beautiful, emotional romance that I will NEVER forget. <br><br>4.5 stars <br><br><i>For more reviews, please visit <a href="http://sinfullysexybooks.blogspot.co.uk/" rel="nofollow noopener">Sinfully Sexy Book Reviews</a> or visit us on <a href="https://www.facebook.com/sinfullysexybookreviews" rel="nofollow noopener">Facebook</a>.</i><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="10904048706988632327" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_548537267" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/548537267" />
    <a title="Christy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/11284813-christy"><img alt="Christy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1594293998p2/11284813.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548537267?book_show_action=true">Feb 28, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Christy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Christy" href="/user/show/11284813-christy">Christy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548537267" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer4554830762811430282"><b>
  <blockquote>I wasn’t always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle first.</blockquote>
</b><blockquote>
<br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/70d357ec-01f5-457d-994a-b0273158ed78_zps383482fa.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411518i/808456.jpg' alt=' photo 70d357ec-01f5-457d-994a-b0273158ed78_zps383482fa.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/><a href='http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/ac71865b-eea4-4578-99af-527fe8156f2f_zps53b19b97.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411518i/808457.jpg' alt=' photo ac71865b-eea4-4578-99af-527fe8156f2f_zps53b19b97.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/></a><br/><br/>Nell Hawthorne and Kyle Calloway have been best friends since the day they were born. They are neighbors, born in the same hospital two days apart, and basically grew up together. Now they are both 16. They both feel more than friendship towards each other, so they start to date. They go from a best friend love, to a romantic love.<br/><br/><b><blockquote>And now we’re learning how to fall in love together. I don’t care</blockquote></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText4554830762811430282" style="display:none"><b>
  <blockquote>I wasn’t always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle first.</blockquote>
</b><blockquote>
<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/70d357ec-01f5-457d-994a-b0273158ed78_zps383482fa.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411518i/808456.jpg" alt=" photo 70d357ec-01f5-457d-994a-b0273158ed78_zps383482fa.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/ac71865b-eea4-4578-99af-527fe8156f2f_zps53b19b97.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411518i/808457.jpg" alt=" photo ac71865b-eea4-4578-99af-527fe8156f2f_zps53b19b97.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><br>Nell Hawthorne and Kyle Calloway have been best friends since the day they were born. They are neighbors, born in the same hospital two days apart, and basically grew up together. Now they are both 16. They both feel more than friendship towards each other, so they start to date. They go from a best friend love, to a romantic love.<br><br><b><blockquote>And now we’re learning how to fall in love together. I don’t care what anyone else says. I love you. I’ll always love you, no matter what happens with us in the future. I love you now and forever.</blockquote></b>
</blockquote><br><br>Kyle is the sweetest guy. Fast forward two years... Nell and Kyle have just graduated high school. They are deciding their futures. Where they are going to go to college, Kyle wants to marry Nell. While on a vacation to a cabin, it starts to storm. A tree falls. Anyone who has read the synopsis knows what happens, doesn’t make it any easier though. Be prepared for some tears. <br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“Don’t leave me.” I barely heard my own voice.<br>“I... I don’t want to,” he whispered. “I love you. I love you.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Nell feels like she is to blame for Kyles death. She can’t cope. She can’t grieve. She can’t let it out.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/bf11a414-2d44-46f2-b7cb-91a00690a92e_zpsdcaf440c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411518i/808458.jpg" alt=" photo bf11a414-2d44-46f2-b7cb-91a00690a92e_zpsdcaf440c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> At Kyle’s funeral, Nell sees Kyle’s older brother, Colton, for the first time since they were kids. Kyle’s brother is the opposite of him. Dark hair, blue eyes, rough around the edges, but he is there for Nell. He’s the only person who tries to comfort her and just lets her deal in peace.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/23cd85b4-2e5d-4d8f-ab62-03eb3f9b3816_zpsb016828e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411518i/808459.jpg" alt=" photo 23cd85b4-2e5d-4d8f-ab62-03eb3f9b3816_zpsb016828e.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>
  <i>“You need to let yourself feel. Feel it, own it. Then move on.”</i>
</b><br><br>Fast forward a few more years... Nell and Colton are both living in NYC. They run into each other for the first time since Kyle’s death. Colton figures out pretty quickly that Nell is still a mess.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/117eeb11-15ff-4e73-b14e-c4d62d42d0f3_zpsf3c39c8c.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411518i/808460.jpg" alt=" photo 117eeb11-15ff-4e73-b14e-c4d62d42d0f3_zpsf3c39c8c.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br> She has never properly grieved, or moved on. Colton wants to be there for Nell. She doesn’t let him at first. As time goes on, he breaks some of her barriers down. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>I want to take her pain.</blockquote>
</b><br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/ad16d3e3-0a98-4a1b-a85b-ab4910805441_zps05dfd326.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411518i/808461._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo ad16d3e3-0a98-4a1b-a85b-ab4910805441_zps05dfd326.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>The main thing Colton tries to get through to Nell is...<br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/c06fb0f9-c763-48ec-8883-82151f2bff7c_zpsfd55af63.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411518i/808462.jpg" alt=" photo c06fb0f9-c763-48ec-8883-82151f2bff7c_zpsfd55af63.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“It’s not okay. You don’t have to be okay.” <br>“What do you want from me?”<br> “I want you to let yourself be broken. Let yourself hurt.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Nell is not the only one dealing with the guilt of the past. Colton has demons of his own. Loved seeing into his past and getting to know what made him the man he is now. Colton knows Nell is special, but its hard for them. He tries to tell her just how he sees her...<br><br><b>
  <i>
    <blockquote>“You’re a lot of things, Nell Hawthorne. You’re complex. You’re cute. You’re lovely. You’re funny. You’re strong. Your beautiful. You’re tortured. You’re hurting. You’re amazing. You’re talented. You’re sexy as fuck.”</blockquote>
  </i>
</b><br><br>Together, they work through their pasts and try to move on from the ghosts. They learn its okay to move on. They lean on each other, on music, and the feelings they have for each other start to surface. <br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/f50366c3-de0e-4e1a-aac2-f7f3a0dbe83a_zpsb4ca2534.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411518i/808463._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo f50366c3-de0e-4e1a-aac2-f7f3a0dbe83a_zpsb4ca2534.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Colt and Nell together... ahh. It was just perfect. It’s like they were meant to be. Things start to go well for the two of them, then something else big happens(I know, as if these two haven’t been through enough already?!?!) that shakes them up. <br><br><br>My emotions were all over the place... I was happy, I was sad, I was heartbroken, It was a beautiful story, there were some really steamy scenes and some heart wrenching scenes. It was kind of all over the place, but in the best way! I loved the music in this story. Music heals the soul, and the play list at the end of the book was amazing! <br>Nell and Colt were beautiful together. This book was heavy. It dealt with some heavy issues, but I absolutely loved it. Nell and Colton’s journey was heartbreaking, but the ending left me happy. This is a wonderful 5 star read, for anyone looking for an emotional heartbreaking story that will leave you with a smile.<br><br><a href="http://s1279.photobucket.com/user/Christyb23/media/7abe40f2-4e7d-4a4e-90c0-47744bda1672_zps3d762fdc.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411518i/808464._SX540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7abe40f2-4e7d-4a4e-90c0-47744bda1672_zps3d762fdc.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="4554830762811430282" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer556525957" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6051974743603325498"><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/WilderFallingIntoYou1TitlebySueBee_zpsbfd3cb79.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388728358i/7911212.jpg' alt=' photo WilderFallingIntoYou1TitlebySueBee_zpsbfd3cb79.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a> <br/><a href='http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Problems/crying2bysb_zpsfa62c16b.gif.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388728358ra/7911213.gif' alt=' photo crying2bysb_zpsfa62c16b.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><b>★★★★1/2! Falling into You. Poignant, beautiful & intense story of love, loss, grief, guilt, healing & second chances!</b><br/><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>Anyone who has ever lost a loved one still a teenager or child knows that gaping void. Yet this story is a reminder that life oftentimes has a way of turning out OK not because of everything that happened, but in spite of it!</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br/>Story is alternating between Nell’s and later Colton’s POV (in first person).<br/><br/><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway</b></i></blockquote></a></span>
  <span id="freeText6051974743603325498" style="display:none"><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/WilderFallingIntoYou1TitlebySueBee_zpsbfd3cb79.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1388728358i/7911212.jpg" alt=" photo WilderFallingIntoYou1TitlebySueBee_zpsbfd3cb79.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a> <br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Problems/crying2bysb_zpsfa62c16b.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388728358ra/7911213.gif" alt=" photo crying2bysb_zpsfa62c16b.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>★★★★1/2! Falling into You. Poignant, beautiful &amp; intense story of love, loss, grief, guilt, healing &amp; second chances!</b><br><b>
  <blockquote>
    <i>Anyone who has ever lost a loved one still a teenager or child knows that gaping void. Yet this story is a reminder that life oftentimes has a way of turning out OK not because of everything that happened, but in spite of it!</i>
  </blockquote>
</b><br>Story is alternating between Nell’s and later Colton’s POV (in first person).<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first. Kyle was my first one true love, my first in every way.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Problems/mirrorbysb_zpse047cb04.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388728358ra/7911214.gif" alt=" photo mirrorbysb_zpse047cb04.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b><br><a>Nell Hawthorne, “Nelly”:</a> daughter of CEO/student-part-time waitress/20 years old/strawberry blond hair/grey-green eyes.</b>
</i><br><br><b>Nell and her first love Kyle grew up together</b>; they were born two days apart, lived next door to each other, their moms were best friends and both families expected them to end up together. At age sixteen they became a couple and had two wonderful years together until that fateful night Kyle tragically died, leaving Nell to fend for herself; In shock, grieving, guilt ridden and trying to make sense of what happened. Such a beautiful innocent love that would never again be.<br><br><b>Nell and Kyle’s brother, Colton</b> see each other at Kyle’s funeral and they apparent that they both feel a special connection, but the timing isn’t right. Fast forward two years when they run into each other in New York, where they both reside.<br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20Heroes/herotattoobysb_zps23502aa5.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388728358ra/7911215.gif" alt=" photo herotattoobysb_zps23502aa5.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>
  <b><br><a>Colton Calloway, “Colt”:</a> Kyle’s older brother/son of Congressman/25 years old/auto body shop owner-musician/black hair/blue eyes.</b>
</i><br><br><b>Colton</b> is handsome, sexy, in control, smart, observant, wise beyond his years. What an amazing hero and precious soul and how his parents could have let him run away at seventeen (a minor!) and never looked for him is perplexing, horrifying, inexcusable and a crime! <br><br>Nevertheless in those eight years since he left he has made a life for himself owning an auto body shop and getting by. As the story unfolds we learn that him getting to that point was horrendous and flecked with danger and he has the battle scars to prove it both inside and out. He has demons and many, many secrets that you are just going to have to read the story to find out.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“He stood more than a foot taller than I did, his shoulders like a football player’s pads, arms corded thick. He was huge, I realized. Kyle had been lean and toned. Colton was… something else. Obviously powerful. Hard. Primal.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>Nell, Nelly</b> has done nothing to deal with her grief, guilt, shame, self-loathing and sorrow in the two years that has passed. Her life is on the brink of spinning out of control. It’s a miracle she is holding it together.<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“You’re a lot of things, Nell Hawthorne. You’re complex. You’re cute. You’re lovely. You’re funny. You’re strong. You’re beautiful.” She seems to be struggling with words and emotions. I keep going. “You’re tortured. You’re hurting. You’re amazing. You’re talented. You’re sexy as f~ck.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>Colt sees Nell</b> and recognizes a lot of warning signs yet he feels this connection, this attraction and this need to save her even though he knows he can’t:<br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“There’s darkness in this girl now. I almost don’t want to get involved. She’ll hurt me. I know this. I can see it, feel it coming. She’s got so much pain, so many cracks and shards and jags in her soul, and I’m going to get cut by her if I’m not careful. I can’t fix her.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br><b>Falling into you is a story of grief, pain, self-loathing, healing, love and second chances</b>. Poignant. Heart wrenching. Beautiful. A must read. Excellent story telling by Jasinda Wilder! <br><br><a>
  <blockquote>
    <i>
      <b>“I’m not just falling in love with you, Nell. I’m falling into you. You’re an ocean, and I’m falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are.”</b>
    </i>
  </blockquote>
</a><br>***<br>Hero rating: 5 stars <br>Heroine rating: 3.5 stars<br>Sex scenes rating: 5 stars<br>Sex scenes frequency: 4.5 stars<br>Storyline concept rating: 5 stars<br>Storytelling skills rating: 5 stars<br>Story ending rating: 4.5 stars<br>Book editing rating (5 = no edits spotted): 4.5 stars<br>************************************************<br><b>Overall rating: 4.5 stars<br><br>Would I recommend this book: Yes.<br>Would I re-read this book: Maybe later.<br>Would I read future books by this author: Yes.</b><br><br><a href="http://s1340.photobucket.com/user/smkarl/media/GIF%20hands/hand3bysb_zpsd891ade9.gif.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1388728358ra/7911216.gif" alt=" photo hand3bysb_zpsd891ade9.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a></span>

    <a title="Katrina Passick Lumsden" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1964146-katrina-passick-lumsden"><img alt="Katrina Passick Lumsden" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416959676p2/1964146.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/572824262?book_show_action=true">Mar 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Katrina Passick Lumsden" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Katrina Passick Lumsden" href="/user/show/1964146-katrina-passick-lumsden">Katrina Passick Lumsden</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17668215-falling-into-you">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer572824262" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8199372873255769316">So. This is NA smut. Not YA smut (which might be illegal? I don't know), not mommy smut. NA smut. <br/><br/>I had <i>thought</i> it was going to be a New Adult <i>story</i> with some steamy scenes, but alas, this book consists of a slew of hastily written, badly paced plot devices weaved awkwardly between sex scenes. The strangest thing is that, even though the sex scenes were (I thought) fairly well-written, they seemed rushed, too. Was the entire thing rushed? Well, we're talking about four or five years and numerous</span>
  <span id="freeText8199372873255769316" style="display:none">So. This is NA smut. Not YA smut (which might be illegal? I don't know), not mommy smut. NA smut. <br /><br />I had <i>thought</i> it was going to be a New Adult <i>story</i> with some steamy scenes, but alas, this book consists of a slew of hastily written, badly paced plot devices weaved awkwardly between sex scenes. The strangest thing is that, even though the sex scenes were (I thought) fairly well-written, they seemed rushed, too. Was the entire thing rushed? Well, we're talking about four or five years and numerous emotional upheavals jammed into 223 pages. Yes, it's rushed. The entire book, summed up in 50 words or less: <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Nell grows up with Kyle, loses her virginity, gets proposed to, Kyle dies, Nell turns into a raging alcoholic and cutter, Colton bangs her a lot and yells at her to cry, Nell miscarries, they "fall into" each other, voila. Problems solved, lots of sex was had, the end. <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span><br /><br />If you enjoy a story to go along with the sex (and if you hate a lot of needless emotional fuckery), steer clear of this book. But if all you're looking for is a quick read about sex, hey, more power to ya.</span>
  <a data-text-id="8199372873255769316" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_565690453" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/565690453" />
    <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p"><img alt="♡Karlyn P♡" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1389996373p2/1131400.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/565690453?book_show_action=true">Mar 19, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♡Karlyn P♡" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♡Karlyn P♡" href="/user/show/1131400-karlyn-p">♡Karlyn P♡</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1131400-karlyn-p?shelf=genre-newadult">genre-newadult</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer565690453" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8336948444257217286"><br/><b>INTO YOU is a dark, steamy, sexy NA romance that aims for heart, punches you in the gut, and then, finally, lifts your spirits sky high. </b><br/><br/>The very first sentence sets the powerful tone for the entire book: <blockquote><i>"I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first."</i> </blockquote>It only took reading that single sentence to convince me to read this book, as I couldn't help but wonder about the brothers and what went wrong. And, what went right. <br/><br/>This is Nell's story, but </span>
  <span id="freeText8336948444257217286" style="display:none"><br /><b>INTO YOU is a dark, steamy, sexy NA romance that aims for heart, punches you in the gut, and then, finally, lifts your spirits sky high. </b><br /><br />The very first sentence sets the powerful tone for the entire book: <blockquote><i>"I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first."</i> </blockquote>It only took reading that single sentence to convince me to read this book, as I couldn't help but wonder about the brothers and what went wrong. And, what went right. <br /><br />This is Nell's story, but it is told over several years and through the alternating POVs of Nell and Colton. For Nell and Colton, survival is about learning how to live life on their own terms, and not through the dreams their parents wished for them as young children. When life crushed their spirits, and their young dreams faded away, pain became their welcomed friend. Emotionally and physically.<br /><br />With this odd connection, Nell and Colton truly understand each other. Through the shared love of music and guitar, they find a friendship and eventually a love that allows them to finally deal with their past. <br /><br />I was surprised how much I liked these two characters together. Fundamentally they were so different, but by the end of the book I couldn't imagine them apart. And for an NA book, this was very steamy. In fact, I would probably call this a straight adult romance. These two burned up a lot of pages! <i>(This author can write some hot steamy scenes. Whew!)</i><br /><br />My issues with the book were small, and they mostly focused around Nell. I did like her and I understood her issues, but I also had to remind myself often that she was young so don't expect her to act like a mature adult. At least not yet. She was an over-thinker and made some questionable choices, which got a bit dramatic for my personal tastes. <br /><br />Colton was a well developed and awesome hero character. For me, he is what made this book so special. He had a rare mix of strength and sensitivity; he was rough and tough but not in a Neanderthal kind of way. He wrote beautiful lyrics, words straight from his heart and soul. But he was fierce and could survive street fighting and protect those around him. <br /><br />FALLING INTO YOU will remind you that life rarely turns out as one expects when they are young, but you can still hope for love and a chance that something special will come of it. And who knows, you might even surpass your wildest dreams. <br /><br /><b>
  <i>((Thanks my GR Friends for the recommendation! Without your reviews, I would have missed this little gem.))</i>
</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="8336948444257217286" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_559932135" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/559932135" />
    <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie"><img alt="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1514769932p2/3275325.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/559932135?book_show_action=true">Mar 13, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ " href="/user/show/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie">Sharon ∞❥ is an emotional book junkie ❥∞ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=kindle-freebies-read">kindle-freebies-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=emotional-angsty-books">emotional-angsty-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3275325-sharon-is-an-emotional-book-junkie?shelf=read-in-2016">read-in-2016</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559932135" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17411641815225925200"><b>Reread 2/6/2016...just as good as the first time!</b><br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br/>With a first line like that, you know this is going to be a tough, gritty, dark book and it definitely is. <br/><br/>Nell grew up with Kyle and they did everything together. It helped that they were neighbors, their mothers were friends and they were born only two days apart. When Nell can finally date, Kyle's best friend asks her out. Unfortunate</span>
  <span id="freeText17411641815225925200" style="display:none"><b>Reread 2/6/2016...just as good as the first time!</b><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br>With a first line like that, you know this is going to be a tough, gritty, dark book and it definitely is. <br><br>Nell grew up with Kyle and they did everything together. It helped that they were neighbors, their mothers were friends and they were born only two days apart. When Nell can finally date, Kyle's best friend asks her out. Unfortunately when she tells Kyle, he freaks out and that leads them both to the conclusion that they have always loved each other <i>as more than friends</i>.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379789157i/519161.png" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's a wonderful first love...full of promise and hope...and happiness. Until one day when things change and Nell will never be the same. <i>Enter Colton</i>, Kyle's older brother, and now Nell will definitely never be the same. <br><br>Both Nell and Colton fight what they feel for each other. They both have been wounded and it takes two years before they see each other again. Nell has spiraled out of control and is barely holding on. Thankfully, Colton recognizes what she is going through and can help her, can help heal her soul. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454818560ra/18017510.gif" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The chapters are spaced out...sometimes in years, sometimes in weeks. At the beginning, Nell and Kyle are only sixteen years old but we move two years ahead fairly quickly. I've always complained about books coming in after a tragedy and missing everything that happened. You don't have to worry about that in this book and I'm not sure I liked it. I know, I know...that's what I get for complaining. It just felt like Kyle's part was a bit choppy and forced. Once Colton comes in, things really smooth out. <br><br>I really enjoyed getting Nell and Colton's POVs. It was intriguing to see the similar things they both went through. I have to admit that I didn't like hearing about Colton's past love life but he should have one too, right? <br><br>I loved how they talked to each other in songs. You always hear how music heals the soul and I really believe that it did in this case. At the end of the book there is a playlist but I really enjoyed these two songs the best:<br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=mrsgIEBwIZM" rel="nofollow noopener">Avett Brothers - I and Love and You</a><br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=O1-4u9W-bns" rel="nofollow noopener">Jason Mraz - I Won't Give Up</a><br> <br>And crazy, hot sex scenes....WOW. This is definitely not a YA book even though the first part makes it feel that way. Colton's got some moves! <br><br>There were a lot of emotional issues that this book deals with. It definitely pulls at your heart strings. And we get some more drama at the end. Not sure how I felt about it and if it was really necessary? What I really wanted was an epilogue...I guess I'm getting spoiled. <br><br>I've heard there's going to be another book, <i>Falling Into Us</i>. JW has said it's not a sequel or a change of POVs but more of an expansion of what everyone went through and more Nell and Colton. It's suppose to come out in July. <br><br>★ I've really been enjoying book trailers that are made by some incredible people. There are a couple out for this book and here's one I really enjoyed:<br><br><a href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=EuQeBZnUq1A" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling Into You book trailer</a><br><br><br>Favorite quotes:<br><br>♥ That note would become my greatest comfort, and the reminder of my deepest heartache.<br><br>♥ “You can’t, Nell. Just…hold my hand. I love you.” <i>(sob!!)</i><br><br>♥ "There’s darkness in this girl, now. I almost don’t want to get involved. She’ll hurt me. I know this. I can see it, feel it coming."<br><br>♥ “It <i>is</i> home. I may sleep upstairs, but this garage is home. More than you know.”<br><br>♦ "I'm a lot of things, Tinkerbell. Sweet ain't one of them."<br><br>♥ “I deserve exactly you,” he cuts in, settling his hands on my hips as I kneel astride his thighs. “Only you. The good and the bad. All you, all beautiful.”<br><br>♥ “I’m not just falling in love with you, Nell. I’m falling into you. You’re an ocean, and I’m falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are. Like you said, it’s scary in a way, but it’s also the most amazing thing I’ve ever experienced. <i>You</i> are the most amazing thing I’ve ever experienced.” <br><br>♥ <i>“All my life it seems <br>I’ve been falling, <br>Failing, <br>Flailing, <br>Barely keeping my head above water. <br>And then one day <br>I saw you <br>Standing beneath a spreading tree, <br>Refusing to weep. <br>But even then I saw <br>The weight of pain hiding in your eyes, <br>And I wished then, <br>There beneath that tree, <br>To take it all away. <br>But I had no words to heal you. <br>I had no words to heal myself. <br>And now that Fate has intervened, <br>Conspired to draw us together, <br>Despite the years between us, <br>Despite the weight of pain <br>Behind both our eyes, <br>Despite the ghosts trailing all around us<br>Like a fog of haunting souls, <br>I’m still trying to find the words to heal you, <br>To take your pain and make it all my own <br>So your beautiful eyes can smile, <br>So you can be at peace. <br>And now that Fate has intervened, <br>Conspired to draw us together, <br>I can’t resist the lure of your eyes, <br>The temptation of your beauty, <br>The siren song of your voice <br>Whispering my name <br>In the dark comfort between my sheets. <br>I can’t resist you, baby, <br>Because I’m falling still, <br>I’m falling into you.”</i></span>
  <a data-text-id="17411641815225925200" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_563466575" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/563466575" />
    <a title="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3716081-it-s-just-me-shelly-b"><img alt="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1374929701p2/3716081.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/563466575?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" class="user" itemprop="url" name="It&#39;s just me Shelly B" href="/user/show/3716081-it-s-just-me-shelly-b">It&#39;s just me Shelly B</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer563466575" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer785727145925563383"><b>"I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first.”</b><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/625904.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book was the absolute saddest "f"ing book I've ever READ!!!! Let me repeat myself.......<b>THE SADDEST book I've EVER read!!!!!</b> This book is going to be very hard for me to review because honestly, I don't like sad books....at ALL!!! So I'm going to start with a general description and then I will get to my feelings on this book.<br/><br/>This book is about Colton and Nell. In the beginning Nell was young</span>
  <span id="freeText785727145925563383" style="display:none"><b>"I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/625904.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was the absolute saddest "f"ing book I've ever READ!!!! Let me repeat myself.......<b>THE SADDEST book I've EVER read!!!!!</b> This book is going to be very hard for me to review because honestly, I don't like sad books....at ALL!!! So I'm going to start with a general description and then I will get to my feelings on this book.<br><br>This book is about Colton and Nell. In the beginning Nell was young, a 16 year old girl, and in love with Kyle but that came to a crashing halt due to a fatal freak accident. Nell being a child herself had a very difficult time dealing with this because not only was Kyle her boyfriend but he had also been her best friend since they were children. <br><br>Colton was Kyle's older brother, he left home after high school due to expectations that he couldn't meet or decided that he wasn't going to meet and made a life of his own on NYC.<br><br>They meet for the first time at Kyle's funeral and they both recognize something in each other....but they aren't quite sure what that is.<br><br><b>“But Colton is…I’m safe with him. He draws the truth out of me. He draws the pain out of me. Colton knows pain. He’s intimately familiar with it. Lives with it. Guilt too.”</b><br><br>So they meet again accidentally in NYC, Colton is a musician and he plays for the love of music not the money and Nell just happens to see him playing in Central Park...and that's when THEIR story begins.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380413729ra/815006.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It's a painful story on both their parts and painful for totally different reasons. They do eventually bare all their emotional baggage to one another..one sad story at a time. They end up being each others true solace and it's beautiful watching it unfold........<b>IF you like sad books!!</b> It really is beautiful watching them heal each other and the music ends up being their escape.<br><br><b>“We understand each other, Nelly. We’ve both lost someone we love. We both have scars and regrets and anger. We can do this together."</b><br><br><b>“...you have to be okay. You have to let yourself heal and move on. You’re stuck in the moment of his death, right now. Locked into a cycle with no way out. You have to break the cycle."</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413729i/815007.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><u>
  <b>My Thoughts</b>
</u><br>Let me start this by saying that this is a great book for people who enjoy THIS kind of book. The book it's self is wonderful, great story line, great characters.....I'm just the WRONG person to read it! I hate sad ass books..........<b>and this is a tear jerker!</b><br><br>Ok enough I'm done.........this book was sad.......sad as hell!!!!!! Nothing and I mean <b>NOTHING</b> went right for these two people!! When you think of a sad book you hope that maybe, just maybe in the end something will work out........and I guess one thing did for them BUT that's ALL.....one thing!!!!! Some of the book didn't even make sense to me because of the high profile careers their parents had...now I know it's fiction and if you write it well enough I don't care if aliens are buying milk at a gas station but if not...it bothers me! This particular thing bothered me, really bad!!! <br><br>I'm going to stop now because part of my issue is I don't like this type of book but I will say that the book was good and I can understand why MANY people enjoyed it, however it just wasn't the book for me. That being said I gave it 3 stars because of personal preference but if you like this style of book 4-5 stars definitely! <br><br>I'm not even going to tell you who recommended this book to me....but you know who you are woman!!!!! This book to me, was her Cam...just so you know:)))))))<br><br>I'm glad I read this book because I know life's not always about roses and rainbows....there is pain and suffering.......but damn!!!!!<br><br>I'm done.............<b>READ it you may LOVE it!!!!!!!</b></span>

<div id="review_562510387" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/562510387" />
    <a title="J" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/10343430-j"><img alt="J" src="https://s.gr-assets.com/assets/nophoto/user/u_50x66-632230dc9882b4352d753eedf9396530.png" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/562510387?book_show_action=true">Mar 16, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="J" class="user" itemprop="url" name="J" href="/user/show/10343430-j">J</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer562510387" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9566673860911540991"><br/><br/>I'm a wreck, I have just been torn down and stripped of all emotions.<br/>I can't even begin to describe how much I loved this book. It went above & beyond any expectation I had. <br/>It is absolutely one of the best books that I've read this year, Jasinda Wilder is brilliant and her writing is just incredible. This book made me feel every word, every touch, every gut wrenching emotion in this story. From the first page to the last sentence.<br/><br/>Falling into You is a beautiful yet Heartbreaking story about a g</span>
  <span id="freeText9566673860911540991" style="display:none"><br><br>I'm a wreck, I have just been torn down and stripped of all emotions.<br>I can't even begin to describe how much I loved this book. It went above &amp; beyond any expectation I had. <br>It is absolutely one of the best books that I've read this year, Jasinda Wilder is brilliant and her writing is just incredible. This book made me feel every word, every touch, every gut wrenching emotion in this story. From the first page to the last sentence.<br><br>Falling into You is a beautiful yet Heartbreaking story about a girl, Nell.<br><br>When Nell's boyfriend Kyle dies suddenly in a tragic accident, Nell is forever changed. <br><br><b>
  <blockquote>"I wanted nothing more than to climb into the box with him and quit breathing, find him in whatever came after life."</blockquote>
</b><br><br><br>At the funeral is where we meet Colton, Kyles older brother. <br>As Nell goes through the days after Kyle's death, Colton is the one that Nell opens up to.<br>There is as undeniable connection between the two that both try to ignore.<br><br>2 Years later in New York City <br>Nell is reunited with Colt<br>Colton realizes that, Nell has never really gotten over Kyle’s death. She still has not grieved for Kyle.<br>She holds on to the pain, guilt and regret by dealing with them in her own unhealthy way.<br>He knows he shouldn’t get involved, but he can’t help himself. He wants to help her.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>~"You need to let yourself feel. Feel it, own it. Then move on."<br>"You make it sound so easy." Bitterness drips from each syllable. <br>"It's not. It's the fucking hardest thing a person can do."~</blockquote>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413590i/814550.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>~"Feel. grieve. Let yourself feel all the anger at the fact that he was taken from you. Feel the loss of him. Feel the sadness and the missing him. Don't block it out, don't cut so it so stops, don't drink yourself numb. just sit and let it all rip you apart And then get up and keep breathing. One breath at a time. One day at a time. Wake up, and be shredded. Cry for a while. Then stop crying and go about your day. You're not okay, but you're alive and you will be okay, someday."~</blockquote>
</b><br><br><br>Colt has his own demons, he is dealing with a past of regret, loss and deals with <br>Together they are painful, mess. <br>They have been through so much hurt, they can see it in each other. <br>He can relate and knows what Nell needs to do to heal her deep wounds.<br><br><br><br>Only when she lets go of her guilt can she slowly start the process of grieving.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>~It's violent, I don't even know how long she sobs. Time ceases to pass, and she cries cries, cries. Clutches me and makes these sounds of a soul being ripped in two, the grief so long denied taking it's toll. ~</blockquote>
</b><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413590i/814551.jpg" width="400" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Their Journey is… I just don't know how to express it to you. It's beyond words. Its an emotion, a feeling, a journey to someplace no one should take. Your heart is pounding and all these emotions rise up the back of your throat only to get stuck.<br> <br><br>Together they slowly heal. <br>They both feel closer to each other than with anyone else before.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>~"I'm still trying to find the words to heal you, <br>To take your pain and make it all my own<br>So your beautiful eyes can smile,<br>So you can be at peace. <br>And now that Fate has intervened,<br>Conspired to draw us together,<br>I can't resist the lure of your eyes,<br>The temptation of you beauty,<br>The siren song of you voice<br>Wispering my name<br>In the dark comfort between my sheets.<br>I can't resist you, baby,<br>Because I'm falling still, <br>I'm falling into you."~</blockquote>
</b><br><br>But with that comes the guilt. The guilt of Kyle <br>However this is real. <br>It's life, it's truth and you won't expect anything else.<br><br><b>
  <blockquote>~"There's no magical healing in this. I won't wake up tomorrow fixed and joyful. I'll still hurt and grieve.<br>But moments like this, with Colton? They make it all bearable. He doesnt fix me, doesn't heal me. He just makes life worthwhile. he helps me remember to breathe, shows me how to smile again. he kisses me and I can forget pain."~</blockquote>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413590i/814552._SY540_.png" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I loved it, couldn't put it down. <br>I haven't cried so hard, so much in one book! <br>The song he wrote in the hospital…. <br>NO words just an absolute blubbering mess. <br><br>Jasinda Wilder AMAZING!! I'm in awe. <br>Her song writing.... It speaks to you. <br>I have read books with references to songs and artists before and never really drew on that. <br>But with Falling into you, it makes you stop and listen. I was on my Itunes listening after each reference and feeling the words. <br>This is a must read for everybody! <br><br> <b>
  <blockquote>~"I'm not just falling in love with you, Nell. I'm falling into you. You're an ocean, and I'm falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are. "~</blockquote>
</b><br><br>Amazing ++ 5 ++ Stars <br><br>Buy it.<br>Read it.<br>Love it.</span>

<div id="review_559520763" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/559520763" />
    <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews"><img alt="Tough Critic Book Reviews" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1345668583p2/5336035.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/559520763?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tough Critic Book Reviews" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tough Critic Book Reviews" href="/user/show/5336035-tough-critic-book-reviews">Tough Critic Book Reviews</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559520763" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12655228047372671865"><b>BOOK TRAILER:</b> <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=cAXSOiKILNQ'>http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=cAXSOi...</a><br/><br/><b><i>Falling Into You</i> will turn you into a sobbing, makeup-less insomniac…with unkempt eyebrows, and snot.</b><br/><br/>We are told from the start that Kyle dies (Stop yelling at me, it’s in the synopsis). No alluding, no inference; it’s black and white…he dies. No beating <i>around</i> the bush; the bush gets its ass kicked! <br/><br/>You’re sad before you even open the book. Then you actually get to <i>know</i> the characters. You fall in love with the characters. Let the free fall </span>
  <span id="freeText12655228047372671865" style="display:none"><b>BOOK TRAILER:</b> <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=cAXSOiKILNQ">http://www.youtube.com/watch?v=cAXSOi...</a><br /><br /><b><i>Falling Into You</i> will turn you into a sobbing, makeup-less insomniac…with unkempt eyebrows, and snot.</b><br /><br />We are told from the start that Kyle dies (Stop yelling at me, it’s in the synopsis). No alluding, no inference; it’s black and white…he dies. No beating <i>around</i> the bush; the bush gets its ass kicked! <br /><br />You’re sad before you even open the book. Then you actually get to <i>know</i> the characters. You fall in love with the characters. Let the free fall begin.<br /><br />Best friends falling in love?? Damn you Jasinda Wilder…damn you. You found my Achilles heel and sliced it with kryptonite. My emotions bled out before I even got to chapter six. You know it’s coming the <i>whole</i> time, but you pray. You pray to God, Buddah, Asian monks, and Obama that it isn’t going to happen. It isn’t. Please don’t let it happen. <br /><br />I even prayed that Jasinda Wilder would eventually jump up and yell, “Syke!! He lives.” <i>That</i> didn’t happen. <br /><br />What did happen was hurt, loss, love, and healing. Colton happened. He never replaced Kyle in my heart, but I accepted that. Nell accepted that. It wasn’t about not hurting. It was about surviving…living. <br /><br />What Nell went through with Kyle is what made her perfect for Colton.<br /><br />In unrelated news, you know what works better than Kleenex to dry tears? Hot passionate sex. When Colton was asleep and she…and it…then he…and…and…OH MY GOD! I’m convinced that sometimes emotional pain is the best aphrodisiac. <br /><br />This was my first time with Jasinda Wilder and she was anything but gentle. There is something about a book that emotionally bleeds you dry that is almost therapeutic. Like an emotional cleanse, cathartic. This was an amazing story to tell and one that will stay with me forever. <br /><br />READ ON!<br /><br />More reviews at <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blogspot.com">http://www.toughcriticbookreviews.blo...</a></span>

<div id="review_548163333" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/548163333" />
    <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag"><img alt="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1410910791p2/8191340.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548163333?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*" href="/user/show/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag">Lise *friends don&#39;t flag*</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=made-me-feel">made-me-feel</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=high-school-sweeites">high-school-sweeites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=friends-to-lovers">friends-to-lovers</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/8191340-lise-friends-don-t-flag?shelf=wrecked">wrecked</a>,

          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548163333" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer14567132906804482448"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411464i/808243._SY540_.jpg' width='300' height='300' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Damn… I love this author. Jasinda Wilder’s writing can draw out every deep-seated emotion and feeling I ever knew existed within me and make it all so painfully beautiful as well as thrilling.<br/>This story starts out with childhood best friends to lovers; Kyle and Nell and their story is so sweet and tragically cut short.<br/><br/>Nell deals with her guilt and sadness in self-destructive ways and it is not until years later when Kyle’s older brother, Colton comes into her life, does she start to heal and for</span>
  <span id="freeText14567132906804482448" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411464i/808243._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Damn… I love this author. Jasinda Wilder’s writing can draw out every deep-seated emotion and feeling I ever knew existed within me and make it all so painfully beautiful as well as thrilling.<br>This story starts out with childhood best friends to lovers; Kyle and Nell and their story is so sweet and tragically cut short.<br><br>Nell deals with her guilt and sadness in self-destructive ways and it is not until years later when Kyle’s older brother, Colton comes into her life, does she start to heal and forgive herself. Colton has some serious issues and secrets of his own but he is well on his road to recovery with help from his love of restoring cars to his music-<br><blockquote>
  <b>“You’re okay, now. You’re okay, now. Just hold on, one more day. Just hold on, one more hour. Someone will come for you. Someone will hold you close. I know, I know. It’s not okay, it’s not all right. But if you just hold on, One more day, one more hour. It will be. It will be.”</b>
</blockquote><br> The healing power of music is a running theme throughout this story and the author does an amazing job of weaving together the words of this book and the lyrics of the songs.<br><blockquote>
  <b>“I could write a song, and her name would be the music. I could sing, strum a guitar, and her body would be the melody"</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Colton and Nell take things slowly as they share their pain of the past and move toward the promise of a future-<br><blockquote>
  <b>“We’re both haunted by the specters of our pasts, but we have to move on sometime and force the voice of our guilt to be silent. Now is that time”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>And… boy do they ever move on, and in and out, and up and down…<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“He pushes in, oh so gently. Oh, god, oh, god, ohmigod. Now his circling fingers are swift and accurate, sending heat through me. I shift and arch, bow my back and roll my hips. So good. So good. I lift up onto my knees and push back, liking the fullness of his finger inside me. Oh, god. “Colton… don’t stop.”</b>
</blockquote><br><br>Yeah… very intense and so full of passion and finally admitted love-<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“I’m not just falling in love with you, Nell. I’m falling into you. You’re an ocean, and I’m falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are”</b>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411464ra/808244.gif" width="450" height="300" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>But fear seeps in again and something happens that could change the course of their love and you will have to read this wonderful book to find out the rest of the story.<br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="14567132906804482448" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/566746821?book_show_action=true">Mar 20, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Heather K (dentist in my spare time)" href="/user/show/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time">Heather K (dentist in my spare time)</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=narrator-so-so">narrator-so-so</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=price-was-right-2-99-or-less">price-was-right-2-99-or-less</a>,
