              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=full-of-angst">full-of-angst</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=everyone-else-loves-it">everyone-else-loves-it</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=new-adult">new-adult</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=m-f">m-f</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13070326-heather-k-dentist-in-my-spare-time?shelf=bye-bye-butt-virginity">bye-bye-butt-virginity</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer566746821" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9759461410506257398">*Audiobook edition*<br/><br/>I DNFed this audiobook at 86%, which was AMPLE time to make up my mind about it. <br/><br/>I bought this book because one of my very few local friends that reads romance was <i>raving</i> about this book. <br/><br/><b>I should have known better. </b><br/><br/>I should have known from all of the dozens of gif-y reviews that this book wouldn't be very good, but this was still a let down. <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17448960.Falling_into_You__Falling___1_' title='Falling into You (Falling, #1) by Jasinda Wilder' rel='nofollow noopener'>Falling into You</a> was like a <b>checklist for everything annoying about romance. </b><br/><br/>The beginning was <i>very</i> YA, and very irritating. First of al</span>
  <span id="freeText9759461410506257398" style="display:none">*Audiobook edition*<br /><br />I DNFed this audiobook at 86%, which was AMPLE time to make up my mind about it. <br /><br />I bought this book because one of my very few local friends that reads romance was <i>raving</i> about this book. <br /><br /><b>I should have known better. </b><br /><br />I should have known from all of the dozens of gif-y reviews that this book wouldn't be very good, but this was still a let down. <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17448960.Falling_into_You__Falling___1_" title="Falling into You (Falling, #1) by Jasinda Wilder" rel="nofollow noopener">Falling into You</a> was like a <b>checklist for everything annoying about romance. </b><br /><br />The beginning was <i>very</i> YA, and very irritating. First of all, the whole sex and virginity issue just came across as ridiculous. I have a thing for the virgin trope in romance (yes, I know it's trite), but I just hate an annoying virgin. Nell was one of those. I have never ever heard of someone just go from only kissing for months to one night jumping to full-on sex, but Nell made it seem like the only way. In fact, the whole relationship with Kyle was so irritating that I wasn't even affected when he finally died (not a spoiler, it's in the blurb). <br /><br />Another thing, because Kyle's death is a thing that readers know is coming, the author kept teasing his death with foreshadowing and "dangerous situations." I kept thinking, "Now this must be when he dies," and then it would be just a random moment where everything turned out okay. <b>I was finally so SICK of being teased as to when Kyle was finally going to kick the bucket that I almost skimmed forward to after his death just to be done with it.</b> And that final death scene was just SOOOO melodramatic. <br /><br />When Nell finally meets Colton years later, it's another disaster. Colton's backstory felt so phony that my eyes were constantly rolling. I'm from the New York area, and the idea that Colton, a rich white boy, would be welcomed into a street gang and then just leave when he felt like it was so fake that it made me want to throw my Kindle. Combine that with a hit-list of classic romance "woe is me" plot elements, and I simply checked out. <br /><br /><b>Misunderstood rich boy! Almost rape! Learning disabilities! Substance abuse! Gangs! Self-harm! <a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[Pregnancy! <a class="jsHideSpoiler spoilerAction">(hide spoiler)</a>]</span></b><br /><br />Just stop, please. Learn some restraint, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6521173.Jasinda_Wilder" title="Jasinda Wilder" rel="nofollow noopener">Jasinda Wilder</a>.<br /><br />In terms of the audio, the narrators were... fine. Nothing special, and certainly not enough to make me want to finish the book. <br /><br />All in all, this was a waste of my time and money. Seasoned romance readers used to something with substance should skip this one. </span>
  <a data-text-id="9759461410506257398" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*" href="/user/show/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty">Farah *Professor Dean&#39;s Beauty*</a>

        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13273769-farah-professor-dean-s-beauty?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548462692" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8877419072265079595"><br/><br/><br/><b>5 heart and Soul Wrenching Stars</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411506i/808402.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>This book BROKE ME!!<br/>I haven't cried whilst reading a book in a long long time... This book had me sobbing at work! Mascara running Sobbing!<br/>This was the most beautifully written book. A very emotional read, a book that will GUTT you but stay with you for a very long time... <br/><br/><br/>Nell Hawthorne had a best friend name kyle Calloway.. Childhood. Friends turned into first loves... Great love.. Love that binds you together till the end...<br/><br/>Until the end is TOO SOON...<br/>One storm</span>
  <span id="freeText8877419072265079595" style="display:none"><br><br><br><b>5 heart and Soul Wrenching Stars</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411506i/808402.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>This book BROKE ME!!<br>I haven't cried whilst reading a book in a long long time... This book had me sobbing at work! Mascara running Sobbing!<br>This was the most beautifully written book. A very emotional read, a book that will GUTT you but stay with you for a very long time... <br><br><br>Nell Hawthorne had a best friend name kyle Calloway.. Childhood. Friends turned into first loves... Great love.. Love that binds you together till the end...<br><br>Until the end is TOO SOON...<br>One stormy August night, Kyle died...<br><br><b>When the light in his eyes went out, the Fire in Nell's heart died.. And part of her died too.</b><br><br>Nell is Numb, she feels the accident was her fault.<br>She meets Colton, Kyles older brother at his funeral. Something about him helps with the pain...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411506i/808403.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Two years later she bumps into him in New York City, where she lives now...<br>They have this pull towards each other.. Like two broken souls drowning, wanting to be saved.. <br><br>Nell has changed... She's broken, empty, sad, wounded.. Just living... But not ALIVE... burrowing the pain deep inside her, numbing herself of the pain, the guilt...to push it away...<br>She drinks, she cuts.. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411506ra/808404.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The pain reminds her of Kyle, afraid if she stops the hurt, she will forget him...<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411506i/808405.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Colton understood her, he had his own type of pain.. He lived and is still living with his pain...<br>He helps Nell accept the pain, accept the hurt, how not to be okay and how to eventually Let it go..<br><br><b>"You need to let yourself feel. Feel it, own it. Then move on.”</b><br><br>Their broken souls bring them together, fighting their feelings for each other.. How can she love her dead boyfriends brother.. How can she feel more for him then Kyle...<br><br><b>"I’m thinking this is the best moment of my life. Honestly. I feel closer to you right now than anyone…ever. I’m thinking…I want to experience moments like this with you forever.”</b><br><br>I absolutely love Colten, he is weak, yet so strong, smart, sexy... And I Love him!<br><br><b>"I’m falling in love with you, Colton. I don’t know if it’s too soon to say that to you, but…it’s true. It’s scary, because I don’t know if everybody is going to understand, but I don’t care right now. I just have to say it to you, because—just because.”</b><br><br>They communicate with beautiful music... Feelings all spilled into songs..<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411506i/808406.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I’m not just falling in love with you, Nell. I’m falling into you. You’re an ocean, and I’m falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are. Like you said, it’s scary in a way, but it’s also the most amazing thing I’ve ever experienced. You are the most amazing thing I’ve ever experienced"</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411506i/808407.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>They still fighting against themselves, in their own ways, with their own ghosts... But together they can help each other. <br>They experience their own kind of loss together... <br><br><b>"But moments like this, with Colton? They make it all bearable. He doesn’t fix me, doesn’t heal me. He just makes life worthwhile. He helps me remember to breathe, shows me how to smile again. He kisses me, and I can forget pain, forget the urges I still have to cut for the pain that erases the emotions. </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411506i/808408.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>"I whisper the words that have come to almost replace I love you between us: “I’m falling into you.”</b><br><br>Everything happens for a reason, and Colton was brought into Nell's life for one.. <b>Not to save her, but to bring her back to Life...</b><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8877419072265079595" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

    <div class="section">
      

<div id="review_558690833" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/558690833" />
    <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie"><img alt="Natasha is a Book Junkie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1585046882p2/9389992.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/558690833?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Natasha is a Book Junkie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Natasha is a Book Junkie" href="/user/show/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie">Natasha is a Book Junkie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=arc">arc</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/9389992-natasha-is-a-book-junkie?shelf=all-time-favorites">all-time-favorites</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer558690833" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer7218417388801593224"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“We’re both haunted by the specters of our pasts, but we have to move on sometime and force the voice of our guilt to be silent.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br/>It’s been three days since I finished reading this book and I am still thinking about it, obsessing about it, catching myself re-reading passages, highlighting new ones. I can honestly say that I never expected to be blown away this completely and I most certainly did not expect to find a new favourite. This story will make you feel so many emotions you won</span>
  <span id="freeText7218417388801593224" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“We’re both haunted by the specters of our pasts, but we have to move on sometime and force the voice of our guilt to be silent.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />It’s been three days since I finished reading this book and I am still thinking about it, obsessing about it, catching myself re-reading passages, highlighting new ones. I can honestly say that I never expected to be blown away this completely and I most certainly did not expect to find a new favourite. This story will make you feel so many emotions you won’t know which way is up and which way is down. Emotional, poignant, exceptionally written, believable… and it comes with the bonus of having by far the hottest sex scene I have ever had the pleasure of reading. And re-reading. And re-reading. As much as this book made me cry and it crushed my heart on so many occasions, it left me deliriously happy because I knew I had found a rare gem.<br /><br />We meet Nell as a young woman living a carefree life – she has a loving family, a blessed childhood, a best friend who has been in her life since they were kids. We watch the friendship between them develop into something more, we watch them fall in love, experience all their firsts, we feel their bond in our hearts and we are giddy about every single happy moment they share as their relationship progresses naturally and effortlessly.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“Nothing mattered but the delirious joy of Kyle, of my first kiss, of making out with my best friend, the only guy I’d ever really cared about.”</i>
</blockquote><br />And then one day Kyle is taken away from her. Suddenly, unexpectedly, cruelly.<br /><br />At Kyle’s funeral, Nell meets his older brother Colton, the black sheep in the family and their pain makes them connect. In their desperation, they share an illicit kiss but Nell is so overwhelmed by grief, loss, regret, sadness, that she pushes him out of her mind and out of her life.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“… it had felt too right, nestled in his arms. Too comforting. Too natural. Too much like home.”</i>
</blockquote><br />Two years later, they accidentally meet again, in a new city, as two adults living away from their families and braving through life as well as they can. Colton has never forgotten the broken young woman who captured his heart at his brother’s funeral, whose pain was so palpable that he wanted nothing more than to take it away from her. The memory of their stolen kiss engraved itself in his soul, marking it and making their chance encounter something he has hoped for ever since she walked away from him that agonising day. It does not take very long for Colton to realise that Nell has never grieved her loss properly. She has bottled all her pain and guilt inside her, deep inside her, never allowing herself to confront her emotions, let them flow through her and excise them that way. She is a ticking bomb and Colton might be the only person in her life equipped to help her face those demons.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“There’s darkness in this girl, now. I almost don’t want to get involved. She’ll hurt me. I know this. I can see it, feel it coming. She’s got so much pain, so many cracks and shards in her soul, and I’m going to get cut by her if I’m not careful.”</i>
</blockquote><br />There is nothing that I could say that would even come close to the intensity of what slowly develops between Nell and Colton. It’s a love story tainted by such unimaginable suffering, by despair from not knowing how to cope with it, by a hopeless tie to a past that should have been cut a long time ago. We feel every one of Nell’s unshed tears, we bleed with them and we desperately wish her to find the happiness she deserves. Colton walks into her life like a knight in shining armour, his own traumatic past being the only weapon that could help Nell.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“I will protect you. From others and from yourself. Always.”</i>
</blockquote><br />They do not just give in to their mutual attraction, they take their time, thread carefully and sensibly, putting Nell’s emotional healing before anything else. She has had two years to allow her guilt to fester inside her and it has become an ugly monster who has the power to shatter her and make her feel worthless. On the other hand, Colton’s persistence and selfless love have the power to pull her out of her dark hole, and open her heart again. By helping her face her pain, Colton is forced to address his own as well, his past becoming the very tool he uses to help Nell.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“We understand each other, Nelly. We’ve both lost someone we love. We both have scars and regrets and anger. We can do this together.”</i>
</blockquote><br />But when they finally succumb to the desire that has been building between them from the moment they laid eyes on each other, it is quite a sight! I’m pretty sure Jasinda Wilder might be responsible for some unexplained seismic activity that occurred the moment I read those scenes! She can write good <i>hot lovin’</i> like nobody’s business!<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>“There’s no start, no stop, no him or me; there is only us, only perfection, only meshed souls and merged bodies and dizzy pleasure.”</i>
</blockquote><br />The writing style is as original as it is effective. Events are narrated at a fast pace – bam, bam, bam – like little daggers stabbing our hearts with every fact that is shared. It holds us captive in the scenes, unable to think of anything else. This is a stunning, heartfelt love story, one that will stay with you for a long time after you finish it. I want to scream from the mountain-tops how much everyone should read this book. This is not an ordinary romance, it is an extraordinary tale of love healing all wounds, no matter how deep they are. An absolute must-read.<br /><br /><blockquote>
  <i>
    <b>“I’m not just falling in love with you, Nell. I’m falling into you. You’re an ocean, and I’m falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are.”</b>
  </i>
</blockquote><br />~ N ♥<br /><br /><a href="http://wp.me/p2YIUs-1A2" rel="nofollow noopener">See this review on my blog!</a> | <a href="http://www.facebook.com/natashaisabookjunkie" rel="nofollow noopener">Follow me on Facebook!</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="7218417388801593224" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559452253" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer11006339870677369630">I rarely do this. In fact I've only ever given 2 other books my <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413143i/813056.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> star rating, but this will be the third for me. <br/><br/>Author provided ARC copy for an honest review. <br/><br/><br/><br/><br/>I am completely <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413143i/813057.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> by this book! <br/><br/>Every emotion I've ever felt was brought forth and it was beyond welcome! <br/><br/>Nell and Kyle's story from the beginning was this beautiful portrayal of young love and all the firsts that people experience. <br/><br/><br/><br/>And then, <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413143i/813058.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><br/>Two years, a proposal and a fallen tree are the end of one chapter in Nell's life and the beginnin</span>
  <span id="freeText11006339870677369630" style="display:none">I rarely do this. In fact I've only ever given 2 other books my <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413143i/813056.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> star rating, but this will be the third for me. <br><br>Author provided ARC copy for an honest review. <br><br><br><br><br>I am completely <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413143i/813057.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> by this book! <br><br>Every emotion I've ever felt was brought forth and it was beyond welcome! <br><br>Nell and Kyle's story from the beginning was this beautiful portrayal of young love and all the firsts that people experience. <br><br><br><br>And then, <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413143i/813058.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Two years, a proposal and a fallen tree are the end of one chapter in Nell's life and the beginning of something altogether more.<br><br><br>All tragic events have a way of making us <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413143i/813059.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> to feelings and life in general. Nell was blind to any emotion other than pain for so long after her loss.<br><br><br><br>Enter Colton and Nell's life is in for an unexpected change. <br><br><br><i>"I'm not just falling in love with you, Nell. I'm falling into you. You're an ocean, and I'm falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are"</i> ~Colton<br>This has to be by far one of the most touching lines I've EVER read in any book. Absolutely beautiful! <br><br>I can't get over the pull that <b>Falling Into You</b> has on me. I'm in serious book hangover from this and I'm not sure if I even care if it passes anytime soon. <br><br><br>I absolutely fucking love this book!!! <br><br><br>My cast: <br><br><br>Colton <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413143i/813060.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Nell <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413143i/813061.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Kyle <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413143i/813062.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I wish I had more words to describe the way that this book has touched me. If you only read one book this year, let it be this one, <b>Falling Into You</b> by the AH-MAZE-BALLS Jasinda Wilder</span>

<div id="review_561875647" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/561875647" />
    <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog"><img alt="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1429608146p2/12994342.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/561875647?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Smitten&#39;s Book Blog" href="/user/show/12994342-smitten-s-book-blog">Smitten&#39;s Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer561875647" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13276840023269624029"><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413498i/814252._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413498i/814253._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>Wow wow, freakin' wow! Oh my life! That was amazing. Intense. Awesome. So inspiring!<br/><br/>I was asked to review this book by the author and I had no idea what I was letting myself in for. Well, actually, that's a lie... I absolutely adored Jasinda Wilder's <i>Wounded</i>, so I knew I liked her writing style and I knew she had the ability to strike a chord in me. But, still... I'm mega excited to say that <i>Falling Into You</i> met my expectations, exceeded them, and some!<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I can tell you what I see. I can t</i></b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText13276840023269624029" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413498i/814252._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413498i/814253._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Wow wow, freakin' wow! Oh my life! That was amazing. Intense. Awesome. So inspiring!<br><br>I was asked to review this book by the author and I had no idea what I was letting myself in for. Well, actually, that's a lie... I absolutely adored Jasinda Wilder's <i>Wounded</i>, so I knew I liked her writing style and I knew she had the ability to strike a chord in me. But, still... I'm mega excited to say that <i>Falling Into You</i> met my expectations, exceeded them, and some!<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I can tell you what I see. I can tell you what I know about you. I can tell how I feel. I can show you what you really are. But arguing with you won't accomplish anything. I think we've both had our share of people trying to fix us. It doesn't work. We can only fix ourselves. Let ourselves heal."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And I am so ridiculously stoked that there is a <i>Falling #2</i>!!!<br><br>But don't worry, this doesn't end with an earth shattering cliffhanger. Don't get me wrong, this WILL shatter your earth! Into a million pieces, more than once. But ohmygod it is sooooo worth it. Colton is so worth it! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>Moments like this, with Colton? They make it all bearable. He doesn't fix me, doesn't heal me. He just makes life worthwhile. He helps me remember to breathe.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This is a pure, no-holds-barred, snotty, all out ugly cry inducing book. I knew what was coming and it still killed me. Jasinda cuts you deep with this one. I have one name for you; Kyle!! <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I know most people would say we're just kids, or to young too know what love is. But screw that. I've known you my whole entire life. We have shared everything together."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>Urgh, Kyle is perfect. He's gorgeous, he's smart, he's loving, he's her first. He's faultless... and you fall in love with him. AND THEN HE DIES!!!! OMG! And that is not a spoiler, because it's in the blurb, so I can say it. Shout it! Scream it because I was sooo angry! Even though I knew it was coming. It was unbearable.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"One breath at a time. One day at a time. Wake up, and be shredded. Cry for a while. Then stop crying and go about your day. You're not okay, but you're alive, and you will be okay, someday."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>So, moving on from Kyle, literally, there's Nell... Nell is wonderful too. She's a sweet, innocent, happy young girl and her world comes crashing down on her when she loses her boyfriend, her best friend and the only person she has ever loved. She takes it badly. She struggles with some very very dark forms of release and her character becomes barely recognisable. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"It helps - "<br>"No it doesn't. It just pushes it away temporarily. Just like the booze."<br>"But I need - "<br>"You need to let yourself feel. Feel it, own it. Then move on."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>So this brings me to Colton! Wooo, 'yay' for Colton, because he is our hero! And what a hero he is. He has all the mandatory qualifications to be your next favourite book boyf'; Tortured past. Uh huh! Muscles covered in ink? Oh yeh! Firey temper and the need to protect damsels in distress? Ding! *drool*<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"They're in your fucking skin, in your soul, like the essence of who they are is imprinted on you so completely they are the very air you breathe, like each molecule of who you are is tangled together. That's love."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>He saves Nell. Well, they help to save one another. Both consumed by their pain, they find solace in each other and learn to deal, together. It's beautifully tragic, but beautiful, all the same.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>She'll hurt me. I know this. I can see it, feel it coming. She's got so much pain, so many cracks and shards and jags in her soul, and I'm going to get cut by her if I'm not careful.</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>And then, if the emotion and the heartbreak and the hotness isn't enough... there's the sex! *fans self* Oooooh my! This is one steamy ass book!<br><br>Do you think I've gushed enough yet? You all neeeeed to read this book. It's a matter of urgency. Well, unless you're not one for a good cry, then absolutely don't read it! :/ BUT, if you don't mind shedding a whole bucket of tears, dive in. <br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"How do you compete with a ghost, Colton?" I whisper the question into a long silence.<br>He shrugs. "I don't know. You don't. You just understand that there's a part of you that you can't give away, because it belongs to a dead person. I don't know."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br>I can not wait for #2!!! I just... ah... I need it, like, now. I hope I don't have to wait too long. I'm going to go and have a cup of tea now.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>
    <i>"I'm not just falling in love with you, Nell. I'm falling into you. You're an ocean, and I'm falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are."</i>
  </b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413498i/814254._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To read more reviews go to my Book Blog: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/">http://smittensbookblog.wordpress.com/</a><br>Follow me on Twitter: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="https://twitter.com/SmittenSC">https://twitter.com/SmittenSC</a><br>Find me on Pinterest: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://pinterest.com/smittensc/">http://pinterest.com/smittensc/</a><br>Join in the chat on Facebook: <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://www.facebook.com/pages/Smittens-Book-Blog/525405204177978">http://www.facebook.com/pages/Smitten...</a></span>

And I know most people would say we're just kids, or </b></i></span>
  <span id="freeText12315554001212603656" style="display:none">4.5 stars.   <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413050i/812830.jpg" alt="Photobucket Pictures, Images and Photos" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Best friends, then lovers, Kyle and Nell were a match everyone saw coming. <br><br>I loved Kyle and Nell's relationship. It was so real. They were just kids, only 16, just discovering what love and lust really meant. Kyle was so sweet, and romantic, but this wasn't an idealized version first love, it was all very real. <br><br><i> <b> "I know we are young. . . . . And I know most people would say we're just kids, or too young to know what love is. But screw that. I've know you my whole life. We have shared everything together. Every important thing in our lives has happened together. . . . And now we're learning how to fall in love together. I don't care what any one else says. I love you. I'll always love you, not matter what happens with us in the future. I love you now and forever. " </b> </i> <br><br><a href="http://s50.photobucket.com/albums/f339/vikkimathews/?action=view&amp;current=imagesCA3ISV2G_zpsd0459fde.jpg" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

</a><br><br>Then just two years later, tragedy takes Kyle from Nell, leaving her in the depths of despair, unable to come to terms with her grief, and guilt. <br><br><i> <b> "I wanted nothing more than to climb into the box with him and quit breathing, find him in whatever came after life. I can see it, feel it coming. She's got so much pain, so many cracks and shards and jags in her soul, and I'm going to get cut by her if I'm not careful. . . . I also know I'm not going to stay way. I'm going to grab onto her and let myself get cut. I'm good at pain. I'm good at bleeding, emotionally, and physically. </a><br><br>I loved Colton. At first I wasn't sure if he might be too broken to help Nelly, but in reality, he was incredibly strong. They were beautiful together. You're an ocean, and I'm falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are." </b> </i> <br><br>My only complaint is that I wish I had just a little bit more. Just a little more of their HEA. They deserve an epic HEA, and I felt just a little bit cheated. <br><br><a class="jsShowSpoiler spoilerAction">(view spoiler)</a><span class="spoilerContainer" style="display: none">[ Colton's song to their lost child killed me. Seriously, broke me. <div id="review_568960330" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/568960330" />
    <a title="Kelena" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7096828-kelena"><img alt="Kelena" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1494750672p2/7096828.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/568960330?book_show_action=true">Mar 23, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kelena" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kelena" href="/user/show/7096828-kelena">Kelena</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7096828-kelena?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7096828-kelena?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7096828-kelena?shelf=fall-head-over-heels">fall-head-over-heels</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer568960330" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer13590632459011648596"><b>
  <i>“Better crazy than broken.”</i>
</b> I wasn’t sure where that came from, hadn’t thought it or meant to say it. <br/><b>“You’re not broken. You’re hurting.”</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414541i/817320._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='350' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>Falling Into You</b> is a beautiful story about a golden son and the troubled son and the girl who wound up loving them both. Circumstance brought them together in different times, one in happy times, the other, in broken times. <br/><br/><b>
  <s>Nell Hawthorne</s>
</b><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379781609i/421717._SY540_.jpg' width='300' height='450' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <s>Kyle Calloway</s>
</b><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414541i/817321._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='600' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><i><b>Kyle and Nell</b> grew up together. Best friends since birth. Once Nell turns 16 and is allowed to st</i></span>
  <span id="freeText13590632459011648596" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>“Better crazy than broken.”</i>
</b> I wasn’t sure where that came from, hadn’t thought it or meant to say it. <br><b>“You’re not broken. You’re hurting.”</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414541i/817320._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Falling Into You</b> is a beautiful story about a golden son and the troubled son and the girl who wound up loving them both. Circumstance brought them together in different times, one in happy times, the other, in broken times. <br><br><b>
  <s>Nell Hawthorne</s>
</b><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1379781609i/421717._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="450" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <s>Kyle Calloway</s>
</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414541i/817321._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i><b>Kyle and Nell</b> grew up together. Best friends since birth. Once Nell turns 16 and is allowed to start dating, Kyle makes his move. These two have the most beautiful, sweet, and innocent relationship. They have loved each other their entire lives… first as friends, then as lovers. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414541ra/817322.gif" width="400" height="261" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Once they graduate from high school, Kyle and Nell start making plans for their future, until tragedy strikes and Kyle is killed while saving Nell’s life.</i> <br><br>That scene was a hard one for me as I could have had a similar outcome in my family with my middle child. Hubs, thank God, hubs heard the crack and screamed bloody murder at our son to move.....and he did.<br><br><i>"Guilt consumes Nell for years. The pain of losing Kyle is too much to bare. Nell was on a downward spiral consumed by grief and suffocated by depression"</i>.<br><br>Enter <b>
  <s>Colton</s>
</b>, Kyle’s older brother. <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414541i/817323._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><b>Colton</b> has a deep soul that has seen much, taken part in a gangster’s life, done bad things. <br><br>You will love Colton. The more his story unfolds, the more your heart will open up to this tattooed, guitar playing, singing guy. He will slowly seep into your veins. Taking up residence. He has such a way with words. <br><br><b>Nell and Colton</b> haven’t seen each other since Kyle’s funeral where they experienced some sort of unspoken bond – until they are reunited by chance on the streets of New York City.<br><b>
  <blockquote>“I wasn’t always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first. Kyle was my first one true love, my first in every way.<br>Then, one stormy August night, he died, and the person I was died with him.</blockquote>
</b><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/547826.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥<br><b>Nell and Colton</b> relationship blossoms even under complicated circumstances. Colton teaches Nell that it’s okay to cry. It’s okay to feel. <br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414541ra/817324.gif" width="400" height="286" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>He helps her breathe again. He helps her let go of her past heartache and find love and passion like she has never experienced. <br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414541ra/817325.gif" width="400" height="237" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>Colton and Nell</b> are two of the most captivating characters, they had me from beginning to end. I loved them individually and together. This book also brings to the forefront coping mechanisms that many people employ in real life. Is it hard to read? Yes, but as I said this book isn’t all heartache. It is also hopeful in many ways. Healing occurs through love and acceptance. <br><br><blockquote>
  <i>I hold her. I don’t tell her it’s okay.<br><b>“Be mad,”</b> I say. <b>“Be hurt. Be broken. Cry.”</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380375051i/729508.jpg" width="300" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></i>
</blockquote><br><br>Realizing that you aren’t alone in depression and destructive behavior may be the first step needed to truly move on. Accepting the truth that they both deserve happiness and love doesn’t come easy to this couple, but it’s beyond beautiful when they do.<br><br><i><b>"Colton</b> didn’t teach me how to live. He didn’t heal the pain. He didn’t make it okay. He taught me how to hurt, how to not be okay, and, eventually, how to let go."</i><br><blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414541i/817326._SY540_.jpg" width="300" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br><br><blockquote>
  <i>You’re okay, now.<br>You’re okay, now.<br>Don’t cry anymore, dry your eyes.<br>Roll the pain away, put it down on the ground and leave it for the birds.<br>Suffer no more, lost child.<br>Stand and take the road, move on and seal the hurt behind the miles.<br>It’s not alright, it’s not okay.<br>I know, I know.<br>The night is long, it’s dark and cruel.<br>I know, I know.<br>You’re not alone. You’re not alone.</i>
</blockquote><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380414541ra/817327.gif" width="400" height="250" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was emotional right through until the end. I didn't smile as anything I read, I didn't laugh... it was just gloom all around and across every page and seriously... I'm feeling drained right now. But still... I was hooked right in.<br><br>Colton is patient. He has his own life he has survived. He is a medicine that Nell needs, but like all medicines, we don’t like taking it. But it will make us feel better.<br><br>He lets Nell be herself ,at the same time he coaxes her into talking about her pain, he in return shares about himself. I loved these parts, the more Colton talked about himself the more I loved him. <br><br><i>"But Colton is ... I’m safe with him. He draws the truth out of me. He draws the pain out of me. Colton knows pain. He’s intimately familiar with it. Lives with it. Guilt too."</i> <br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414541i/817328.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>I need to know what’s driving this girl. What’s devouring her. </i><br><b>“Tell me.”</b> I whisper the words to her, rough and raw in the unlit bathroom, gray dawn filtering through dirty glass. <br><br><b>“He’s dead.” <br><br>“That’s not enough.” <br><br>“It’s everything.”</b><br> <blockquote>
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414541i/817329._SY540_.jpg" width="260" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</blockquote><br>♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥<br><br>It’s both heartbreaking and hopeful. Two damaged souls that meet under the most horrifying circumstance and share a connection, but don’t act on it. When they meet again thinking neither of them deserve love or happiness the story just gets better and I couldn’t stop reading it.<br><br><br><b>
  <blockquote>“I’m not just falling in love with you, Nell. I’m falling into you. You’re an ocean, and I’m falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are. Like you said, it’s scary in a way, but it’s also the most amazing thing I’ve ever experienced. You are the most amazing thing I’ve ever experienced.”</blockquote>
</b><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414541i/817330._SX540_.jpg" width="400" height="350" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br><i>"He’s raw and rough and kind and smart and nearly illiterate<br>but so brilliant and so talented and so fucking hot it’s absurd and he’s mine."</i><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414541i/817331._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="600" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥♫♥<br>Music played a big part in this book as well. It gave a voice to the pain. A voice to the emotions that were bottled up deep inside. The songs really got to me and I cried while reading almost every one.<br><br>This book is not rainbows and butterflies. It is not your typical love story. It is dark, emotional and deep. It is not only tragic and completely heartbreaking, but it is also filled with hope and love. Hope that you can find the strength to move on after a devastating loss and learn to love again<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380414541i/817332.png" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>
  <a data-text-id="13590632459011648596" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

Wait, what do you mean there are other things in this book except for the sex scenes? Oh, now I remember... you must be talking about that underage illegal drinking scene that happened. No? Is it maybe the countless number of scenes in which the main character bites her lip? Not that one either? Then you must be talking about that scene in which we miraculously fin</span>
  <span id="freeText1537341562551425209" style="display:none"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473511711i/20474529.jpg" width="280" height="60" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It really could happen to anyone!<br><br>Jasinda Wilder did a great job of including those 3 "normal" scenes in this short book about sex... Wait, what do you mean there are other things in this book except for the sex scenes? Oh, now I remember... you must be talking about that underage illegal drinking scene that happened. No? Is it maybe the countless number of scenes in which the main character bites her lip? Not that one either? Then you must be talking about that scene in which we miraculously find out that the two main characters are exceptional singers whose voices are like a damn angel choir. What do you mean, it's not this one either? The only thing that's left is the fact that Colton is in a gang? Like, he calls his gang friends "homies"... I honestly get <i>shivers</i> just by imagining how <i>dangerous</i> this guy is. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473510972i/20474414.jpg" width="400" height="200" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>To be honest, there's this particularly wonderful and touching scene in which Nell gives Colton a handjob while he sleeps, just a day after they saw each other again. Aww, I know, this one warms my heart too! <br><br>Overall, this is a really fantastic book - you will learn so many things from it. For example, how to wish that an already dead character dies again just because of how annoying he was during his life, or that after someone you love dies destructive behavior is, really, the only normal way for you. I know, I know, this one was a real tear-jerker! <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1473511521i/20474496.jpg" width="330" height="190" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_563673820" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/563673820" />
    <a title="Jen " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5962787-jen"><img alt="Jen " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1563496869p2/5962787.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/563673820?book_show_action=true">Mar 17, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jen " class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jen " href="/user/show/5962787-jen">Jen </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=contemporary-romance">contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5962787-jen?shelf=tissues-required">tissues-required</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer563673820" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15217933238965553873"><i>
  <b>"I'm not just falling in love with you, Nell. I'm falling into you. You're an ocean, and I'm falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are. Like you said, it's scary in a way, but it's also the most amazing thing I've ever experienced. <i>You</i> are the most amazing thing I've ever experienced."</b>
</i><br/><br/>Damn, I love this book! Not like in a "it's really great" or "I was pleasantly surprised" kind of way. No, I love this book! Colt and Nell are both hurting, scarred and in need of a safe haven. The simp</span>
  <span id="freeText15217933238965553873" style="display:none"><i>
  <b>"I'm not just falling in love with you, Nell. I'm falling into you. You're an ocean, and I'm falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are. Like you said, it's scary in a way, but it's also the most amazing thing I've ever experienced. <i>You</i> are the most amazing thing I've ever experienced."</b>
</i><br /><br />Damn, I love this book! Not like in a "it's really great" or "I was pleasantly surprised" kind of way. No, I love this book! Colt and Nell are both hurting, scarred and in need of a safe haven. The simple fact that these characters were there for each other and became the other's safe place, combined with the scorching heat, made my heart do a little happy dance. There's nothing mundane about this story. There's BIG feelings and BIG love and I wouldn't want it any other way.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15217933238965553873" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_560802616" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/560802616" />
    <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads"><img alt="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1380942477p2/4197769.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/560802616?book_show_action=true">Mar 14, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jacqueline&#39;s Reads" href="/user/show/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads">Jacqueline&#39;s Reads</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=5-stars-favorites">5-stars-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=6-stars-top-favorites">6-stars-top-favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4197769-jacqueline-s-reads?shelf=freebie">freebie</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer560802616" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10668221631434729644"><b>NOW FREEEE - <a target='_blank' rel='noopener nofollow' href='http://amzn.to/1Erifzt'>http://amzn.to/1Erifzt</a> and AUDIO is $1.99</b><br/><br/><b>5 Stars!!!!!!</b><br/><br/><b>
  <i>I’m not just falling in love with you, Nell.<br/><br/>I’m falling into you.</i>
</b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413341i/813732.jpg' width='250' height='375' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b><i>Falling Into You</i> is a Fabulous. Fantastic. Swoon-Worthy. Emotional. Incredible. READ!!!</b><br/><br/>I want to kick myself in the butt for waiting so long before I picked up this book. One of the reasons why I waited so long was because I wasn’t a fan of the blurb. Even though lately I have been liking depressing reads, I just didn’t want to get into the whole brother-death t</span>
  <span id="freeText10668221631434729644" style="display:none"><b>NOW FREEEE - <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://amzn.to/1Erifzt">http://amzn.to/1Erifzt</a> and AUDIO is $1.99</b><br><br><b>5 Stars!!!!!!</b><br><br><b>
  <i>I’m not just falling in love with you, Nell.<br><br>I’m falling into you.</i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413341i/813732.jpg" width="250" height="375" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b><i>Falling Into You</i> is a Fabulous. Fantastic. Swoon-Worthy. Emotional. Incredible. READ!!!</b><br><br>I want to kick myself in the butt for waiting so long before I picked up this book. One of the reasons why I waited so long was because I wasn’t a fan of the blurb. Even though lately I have been liking depressing reads, I just didn’t want to get into the whole brother-death thing, but <b><i>Falling Into You</i> was JUST.SO.MUCH.MORE.</b><br><br>[Summary/Blurb]<br><br>The summary is basically everything you needed to know and after finishing my read, I realized how perfect the blurb was. Nell fell in love with her best-friend, Kyle and then one day he dies. Nell is having a hard time grasping Kyle’s death. Kyle has an older brother, Colton, who Nell hasn’t really interacted with since Colton moved away years ago. Because of similar pains, Colton helps Nell heal her wounds.<br><br>[My review]<br><br><b>
  <i>Falling Into You</i>
</b> was perfectly written. I really loved the writing style because Jasinda Wilder wrote in chronological order and there was ZERO FLASHBACKS. I can’t STRESS how much I love that. Because Wilder wrote it in chronological order, I really did get to understand Klye’s and Nell’s relationship. <br><br>A lot of times when you read a book where the Heroine has to deal with a past pain, it’s usually a big mystery and when you do find out what it is, you can’t really empathize because you as the reader ,didn’t get a chance to feel what the Heroine is feeling. However,<b>I.FELT.NELL’s.PAIN</b> to the fullest. <br><br>[Disclaimer]<br><br>Many readers don’t want to read a book where a guy dies, I get it, but <i>Falling Into You</i> isn’t just about that. Yes, you do like Kyle and yes, it’s sad, but you are so consumed with the story, his death is just a side note. I hope that makes sense, because I don’t want Kyle’s death to be a deterrent to why people don’t pick up this book. <br><br>[Nell]<br><br>I 100% LOVED Nell. She is beautifully damaged and a perfect Heroine in my opinion. I get her, I understand her, and like I said, I feel for her. Wilder paints a wonderful, yet broken picture of Nell and you see her starting out as this young teenager and slowly growing into a woman but still trying to figure out what to do with herself. <br><br><b>
  <i>There’s darkness in this girl, now. I almost don’t want to get involved. She’ll hurt me. I know this. I can see it, feel it coming. She’s got so much pain, so many cracks and shards and jags in her soul, and I’m going to get cut by her if I’m not careful. </i>
</b><br><br><br>[Colton]<br><br><b>I 100% LOVE Colton, yep, he’s up there in my book boyfriends, next to the Travis, next to the Christian and next to the Gideon.</b> Yes, bring on the tattoos, bulky built, dominate, ruff-around-the-edges, scruffy, alpha male PLEASE! In the beginning you don’t really get a clear picture of who Colton is, but slowly as his character develops, you form an attachment to him and yes, fall in love with him.<br><br>Taking a moment to <b>**SWOON**</b> <br><br>[My version of Colton]<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413341i/813733._SY540_.jpg" width="250" height="375" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>I don’t deserve her, but I’m an asshole, a selfish bastard, so I take what I can get from her, and try to make sure I give her the best I’ve got.</i>
</b><br><br>[Overall]<br><br><i>Falling Into You</i> is written from both Colton’s and Nell’s POV. The read is very fast pace and at times I wonder if it could have been a little longer, but overall, I think the length and tone was just right for me. There’s plenty of character development and a lot of emotional baggage that comes out. If you aren’t into emotional books then this isn’t for you.<br><br>There were no annoying points and almost everything that needed to be said was said at the right time. Overall the dance between tension and emotional revealing was (and I’ll say it again) perfect. The book is pretty steamy, but it doesn’t take away from the story, in all honestly it enhances it.<br><br><b>
  <i>Compassion and pity are not the same: pity is looking down on someone, feeling sorry for them and offering nothing; compassion is seeing their pain and offering them understanding.</i>
</b><br><br>I’ve never dealt with the loss of anyone that close to me, but Nell’s and Colton’s emotions seem very realistic. I simply couldn’t put the book down.<br><br>I loved <b>Falling Into You</b>, it’s a type of read where I’ll definitely read again (I kind of wanted to after I just finished it). I recommend this book for those who like emotional, yet moving stories that will make you appreciate life. <br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/17448960.Falling_into_You__Falling___1_" title="Falling into You (Falling, #1) by Jasinda Wilder" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/books/1363055080s/17448960.jpg" alt="Falling into You (Falling, #1) by Jasinda Wilder" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><a href="http://www.amazon.com/gp/product/B00BUPMC8C/ref=as_li_qf_sp_asin_tl?ie=UTF8&amp;camp=211189&amp;creative=373489&amp;creativeASIN=B00BUPMC8C&amp;link_code=as3&amp;tag=jacqsread-20" rel="nofollow noopener">AMAZON</a><br><br>For more reviews, visit <a target="_blank" rel="noopener nofollow" href="http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/">http://jacquelinesreads.blogspot.com/</a></span>

<div id="review_558603713" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/558603713" />
    <a title="Lisa" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/13978199-lisa"><img alt="Lisa" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1412857185p2/13978199.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/558603713?book_show_action=true">Mar 11, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lisa" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lisa" href="/user/show/13978199-lisa">Lisa</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=angsty-romance">angsty-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review">arc-given-to-blog-for-honest-review</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=fav-books-of-all-time">fav-books-of-all-time</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=ugly-cry">ugly-cry</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/13978199-lisa?shelf=read-in-2013">read-in-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer558603713" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer8086851835227884689">*ARC given to blog for honest review*<br/><br/>5+++ <b>“Oh god, oh god…<i>ohmigod</i>”</b> Kisses! One of the best books I’ve read this year and a new addition to my favorite books of all time.<br/><br/>Gutted. Floored. Emotionally wrung dry. And ya know what? I’d read it all over again in a heartbeat. How does an author literally break my heart and I can sit here and say I loved every second of it? Because it was one of the most beautifully written books I have ever read.<br/><br/>Falling Into You topped the charts for me – you can’t rea</span>
  <span id="freeText8086851835227884689" style="display:none">*ARC given to blog for honest review*<br><br>5+++ <b>“Oh god, oh god…<i>ohmigod</i>”</b> Kisses! One of the best books I’ve read this year and a new addition to my favorite books of all time.<br><br>Gutted. Floored. Emotionally wrung dry. And ya know what? I’d read it all over again in a heartbeat. How does an author literally break my heart and I can sit here and say I loved every second of it? Because it was one of the most beautifully written books I have ever read.<br><br>Falling Into You topped the charts for me – you can’t read the synopsis and not know what you’re getting yourself into. You’re signing up to have a nice long ugly cry. It happens. We fall in love with characters, it’s impossible not to – and anyone that says they didn’t fall in love with Kyle is a crazy person.<br><br>Nell Hawthorne &amp; Kyle Calloway are best friends, born two days apart, grew up just down the street from each other, they’ve been inseparable since birth. It’s presumed, but not assumed, that they would eventually have a romantic relationship, but at 16 they finally figure it out…and that’s where the magic begins. New love…first love…first everything, it’s the stuff that makes your heart flutter, and mine did with Nell and Kyle.<br><br><b>“Kyle was my first one true love, my first in every way.”</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380398309ra/769628.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fast forward two years, Nell &amp; Kyle are 18, about to graduate high school and making some huge decisions…trying to figure out what they want while still keeping their relationship intact, everything is changing so it’s either adapt and grow with it or lose something precious. Unfortunately something precious is lost but it’s not due to their choices. <b>**Be Prepared – it’s not <i>will</i> you ugly cry, it’s <i>how long</i> will you ugly cry**</b><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/457822.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>“It wasn’t a tear. I wouldn’t cry. Couldn’t. To let it go would be to open my soul. It would never stop. I would break…just shatter. The liquid on my cheek was blood, surging out from my ripped and tattered heart.” </b><br><br>It’s very conflicting to love and hate the fact that you are crying…but I did. I hated what was happening, I hated the loss of Kyle, I hated every tortuous second but the writing was beautiful. Gorgeous. Flawless. I felt every emotion from Nell…it hurt like <b>HELL</b> but just writing about it now and recalling what happened makes me cry!<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/522916.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Enter Colton Calloway, Kyle’s older brother, at the funeral…Nell knows of him but doesn’t really know him…they have some moments, once again the pain is palpable – because they are both hurting <b>so</b> much. Nell prefers the physical pain to the emotional pain, she feels unworthy that she is still alive while Kyle isn’t. There is a break of two years and they reconnect…by chance. It doesn’t end there…there’s a pull and a draw coming from both of them – as much as they want to ignore it, they don’t…they can’t.<br><br><b>“You’re a lot of things, Nell Hawthorne. You’re complex. You’re cute. You’re lovely. You’re funny. You’re strong. You’re beautiful.” She seems to be struggling with words and emotions. I keep going. “You’re tortured. You’re hurting. You’re amazing. You’re talented. You’re sexy as fuck.”</b><br><br>More conflicting emotions because after all their pain, there is a chance for them to be happy, and with probably the only other person on the planet that can truly understand the pain that you’re experiencing. But those ghosts don’t go away and the opportunity for joy almost never happens…but thank God, it does. They deal with it together, cope together, heal together.<br><br><b>“I can tell you what I see. I can tell you what I know about you. I can tell you how I feel. I can’t show you what you really are. But arguing with you won’t accomplish anything. I think we’ve both had our share of people trying to fix us. It doesn’t work. We can only fix ourselves. Let ourselves heal.”</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380413011i/812668.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I <b>loved</b> Nell &amp; Kyle, a lot, don’t get me wrong…but Nell and Colton together were <b>
  <i>amazing</i>
</b>. Even thru their poor shattered broken hearts, seeing them learn to love again, watching both of them open up, more emotions, ugh – and there I go with the tears again. They made my heart flutter, my pulse race, and brought peace to my soul because I <i>needed</i> them to be whole again. And in the end…I got what I needed.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/526116.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The book is mainly from Nell’s perspective, but we did get a few chapters from Colton…I liked the alternating POV’s, sometimes it’s nice to know everything the characters or thinking but being let in their thoughts in some places and not in others kept things interesting. And the way she split it up and always let you know whose brain you were in was really clear and concise. <br><br>This book was above and beyond an insane…intense….<br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/419639.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>It blew my mind, shattered my expectations and just absolutely floored me. Drop whatever you are reading and read Falling Into You ASAP!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="8086851835227884689" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_559436426" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/559436426" />
    <a title="Tammy  Zautner" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6539323-tammy-zautner"><img alt="Tammy  Zautner" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1461189789p2/6539323.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/559436426?book_show_action=true">Mar 12, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tammy  Zautner" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tammy  Zautner" href="/user/show/6539323-tammy-zautner">Tammy  Zautner</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6539323-tammy-zautner?shelf=6-stars">6-stars</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6539323-tammy-zautner?shelf=worthy-reads-of-2013">worthy-reads-of-2013</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer559436426" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15733628479031549381"><b> 6 Stars</b><br/><br/>"I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first."<br/><br/>Um, wow! I am a bit speechless right now. I did not read the blurb for this book. Jasinda asked Kim and I to read and review, the cover looked awesome so I said ok and just dived right in. Glad I had no clue what the book was about because at about 26% Jasinda rocked my world and handed me my shredded heart on a silver platter. If I had known what I knew at that point beforehand I don’t th</span>
  <span id="freeText15733628479031549381" style="display:none"><b> 6 Stars</b><br /><br />"I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first."<br /><br />Um, wow! I am a bit speechless right now. I did not read the blurb for this book. Jasinda asked Kim and I to read and review, the cover looked awesome so I said ok and just dived right in. Glad I had no clue what the book was about because at about 26% Jasinda rocked my world and handed me my shredded heart on a silver platter. If I had known what I knew at that point beforehand I don’t think I would have had the same reaction or connection to Kyle. I loved that I was so clueless. I loved that my heart dived to my stomach and my eyes filled with big fat tears that just kept right on pouring through half the book and then some. Falling into You was filled with a roller coaster of emotions, including angst, love, fear, pain, guilt, and a glimmer of hope.<br /><br />I adored Nell and Kyle together. I loved that they had been best friends since they were wee tots. Their love was strong and it was a true love, well as true as it could be at 16-18 years old. I found myself smiling over the romantic things Kyle said and did. I was completely and utterly invested in them. Then out of nowhere, Nell’s world turned upside down and fell out from beneath her and so did mine. I hurt with her. My heart shattered into pieces for her and Kyle. I felt as broken as Nell did. I wondered how the author was going to pull off her healing, how she would help her move forward past the grief, the pain, the guilt, the loneliness. <br /><br />“It wasn’t a tear. I wouldn’t cry. Couldn’t. To let it go would be to open my soul. It would never stop. I would break…just shatter. The liquid on my cheek was blood, surging out from my ripped and tattered heart.”<br /><br />Enter Colton Calloway. Colt was perfection wrapped up in his own pain, his own loss. He had walls wrapped so high around his heart, allowing no one in until Nell. Colt lived the life of a bad boy until a few tragedies struck and he found his self-navigating the “straight and narrow.” He no longer wanted a life that offered him nothing but destruction. Colt understood the pain and the guilt that riddled Nell. He pushed her, but not so hard that he couldn’t catch her when she fell. My heart ached so many times for this misguided man who showed tremendous loyalty, protectiveness, and vulnerability. His choices were not always smart, but they shaped him into the man who will stand strong next to Nell offering her the strength and love she will need to move forward. <br /><br />“But Colton is…I’m safe with him. He draws the truth out of me. He draws the pain out of me. Colton knows pain. He’s intimately familiar with it. Lives with it. Guilt too. Colton has secrets, and I want to know them all.”<br /><br />I was blown away by Colton and his determination to love Nell while helping her face current day reality. Although, he moved slow he didn’t enable her, in addition, he also didn't allow her to continue on a destructive path. Colt helped find the courage to search within herself to find the forgiveness she needed from herself in order to move past the guilt she had been holding on to for years. Their relationship was so hard to read at some points. The pain just radiated off the page, it was raw and intense. The need they felt for each other was agonizing and all-consuming at times. Their chemistry was off the charts, and scared the living day lights out of Nell, making her doubt everything she knew with Kyle. Colt and Nell struggled, emotionally and mentally she was a train wreck, but he stood next to her side through it all. Each felt their own brand of guilt as they journeyed through the pain.<br /><br />“Feel. Grieve. Let yourself feel all the anger at the fact that he was taken from you. Feel the loss of him. Feel the sadness and the missing him. Don’t block it out, don’t cut so it stops, don’t drink yourself numb. Just sit and let it rip you apart. And then get up and keep breathing. One breath at a time. One day at a time. Wake up, and be shredded. Cry for a while. Then stop crying and go about your day. You’re not ok, but you’re alive, and you will be ok, someday.”<br /><br />“We understand each other, Nelly. We’ve both have scars and regrets and anger. We can do this together.”<br /><br />This is my first read by Jasinda Wilder, and boy did she wreck my world while slowly placing it all back together piece by piece. This was a story of how light can shine through the bitter darkness and offer a second chance at life. I really enjoyed her writing style, her characters and story line were so well developed. I will definitely search out more reads by her. I also enjoyed the alternating point of views, it helped keep me well invested in them and their outcome. I highly recommend this book and author!<br /><br />Thank you to Jasinda Wilder for the opportunity to take this wild ride with Nell and Colton. Author provided an ARC of Falling into You in exchange for an honest review.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15733628479031549381" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
