<span id="freeTextContainer15610012861273960998">5 soul bearing, heart breaking stars.<br/><br/>"I'm not just falling in love with you, Nell. I'm falling into you. You're an ocean, and I'm falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are." <br/><br/>Jasinda Wilder, knows how to write emotion - gritty, sad, heart achingly moving emotion. I was glued to the pages, I could not put this story down, this was an unforgettable reading experience. This book should come with a warning ~ or free tissues! There was lots of Lisa tears. I was a big, messy pile of girly emoti</span>
  <span id="freeText15610012861273960998" style="display:none">5 soul bearing, heart breaking stars.<br /><br />"I'm not just falling in love with you, Nell. I'm falling into you. You're an ocean, and I'm falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are." <br /><br />Jasinda Wilder, knows how to write emotion - gritty, sad, heart achingly moving emotion. I was glued to the pages, I could not put this story down, this was an unforgettable reading experience. This book should come with a warning ~ or free tissues! There was lots of Lisa tears. I was a big, messy pile of girly emotion most of the way through this story ... So be prepared.<br /><br />The author weaves a mixture of Light and dark, Love and hate, Pain and joy, Past and future, Suffering and healing. All put together in a gorgeously written, relatively short book.<br /><br />From the beginning the reader is thrown into the gorgeous first love of Nell and Kyle ~ a beautiful friendship that grows into true soul mate love, it was moving and realistic. I was sold straight away I was instantly swept up in the story, then boom heartache, grief, bereavement ~ intense and dark. The story then follows the lives of Colton and Nell ~ The Journey of Nell grieving her past to take hold of her future. Colton comes like a breath of fresh air, and although I didn't think it possible I fell in love all over again. <br /><br /> Their is a depth to this story that is sincere. Undoubtably I fell in love with this story and the characters. Although this book is by no means easy ~ if angst, heartache and love is your thing, then don't delay. <br /><br />"I walked the steps to her apartment with the window by the shore<br />And saw her curled on the tile through a crack in the door<br />I've been searching for the words I don't know how to say<br />I've been searching for the words to make it go away<br />I spent all of last night and the night before that<br />With my feet in the sand and the wind on my back<br />Watching a ship sail out to a blue wide sea<br />There must be more than this with a kiss we can't see" ~ 'can't break her fall' Matt Kearney <br /><br />5 Nelly and Colton stars ... </span>

<div id="review_1882586891" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1882586891" />
    <a title="Dilek VT" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt"><img alt="Dilek VT" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1448923258p2/49572641.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1882586891?book_show_action=true">Jan 25, 2017</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Dilek VT" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Dilek VT" href="/user/show/49572641-dilek-vt">Dilek VT</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=death">death</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=deep-emotions">deep-emotions</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=insta-lust">insta-lust</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=drama-and-healing">drama-and-healing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=steamy-hot">steamy-hot</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=love-second-chance">love-second-chance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=sad-story">sad-story</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=second-chances-in-life">second-chances-in-life</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=abuse-violence">abuse-violence</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/49572641-dilek-vt?shelf=painful-situation">painful-situation</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1882586891" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12598924626330959976"><b>
  <i>I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first. </i>
</b><br/><br/>This is a tough book to read. Beautiful, nevertheless...<br/><br/>Nell and Kyle are best friends. Then, they fall in love with each other when they are 16. <br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1485334164i/21804310.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>First true love. First everything…<br/><br/> <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1485334164i/21804311.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/><b>
  <i>I know we’re young. And I know most people would say we’re just kids, or to young too know what love is. But screw that. I’ve known you my whole entire life. We have shared everything together. Every important th</i></b></span>
  <span id="freeText12598924626330959976" style="display:none"><b>
  <i>I wasn't always in love with Colton Calloway; I was in love with his younger brother, Kyle, first. </i>
</b><br><br>This is a tough book to read. Beautiful, nevertheless...<br><br>Nell and Kyle are best friends. Then, they fall in love with each other when they are 16. <br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1485334164i/21804310.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>First true love. First everything…<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1485334164i/21804311.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>I know we’re young. And I know most people would say we’re just kids, or to young too know what love is. But screw that. I’ve known you my whole entire life. We have shared everything together. Every important thing in our lives has happened together. And now we’re learning how to fall in love together.</i>
</b><br><br>Everything seems to be perfect between these two teenagers, until Kyle dies in a tragic accident when he is 18, leaving Nell feeling guilty and broken.<br><br>Kyle’s brother Colton was away for many years. He loved a girl, India, very much but he lost her too. He is a suffering man, as well.<br><br>Colton and Nell meet in Kyle’s funeral after a lot many years. There is a strange spark between the two of them. They feel it but both are too broken to do anything about it so 2 years pass without contact.<br><br>After 2 years, fate somehow brings them together again. They get closer and closer slowly and still don’t know what to do with the strong attraction between them. They are attracted to one another but they are also haunted by past ghosts.<br><br>Colton sees that Nell has never let herself grieve for the loss of Kyle because she is afraid of being shredded into pieces. Therefore, she doesn’t live much, she just exists. She replaces pain with pain, by physically hurting herself.<br><br><b>
  <i>I notice her hands are clutched around the opposing wrists, nails digging in deep, hard, scratching. Pain to replace pain. <br><br>***<br><br>“You need to let yourself feel. Feel it, own it. Then move on.” </i>
</b><br><br>FALLING INTO YOU starts with the story of Kyle and Nell and continues with the story of Colton and Nell. Because Kyle and Colton were brothers, that was a hard pill to swallow for me as well as for the two of them. <br><br><b>He wants me, but won’t give in to it. Which I get, I really do. <br>He’s my dead boyfriend’s brother. <br>It’s just…wrong. <br><i>How did you two meet? <br>Oh, we met at his brother’s funeral. His baby brother, my first love. </i><br>Awesome.</b><br><br><b>
  <i>***<br><br>And I know he wants this as much as I do, and we’re both conflicted about it.<br><br>***<br><br>I search his eyes, and see my emotions reflected back at me: conflicted desire. </i>
</b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1478750372i/21107924.jpg" height="550" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>I struggled as they struggled but the writer gives that period of feeling guilty and contradicted in a very realistic way. Nothing happens too fast. It happens gradually. Of course, I would have preferred Colton not to be related to Kyle, but, alas, he was. Despite this great disadvantage, he was exactly the person Nell needed. That is why, in spite of their ghosts, they tried to stick together, helping each other to heal and feel again.<br><br> <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1485334164i/21804312._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><b>
  <i>I’m safe with him. He draws the truth out of me. He draws the pain out of me. Colton knows pain. He’s intimately familiar with it. Lives with it. Guilt too. Colton has secrets, and I want to know them all.</i>
</b><br><br>It is a painfully beautiful story. Their falling into each other and finding peace and moments of happiness within each other's company was worth reading.<br><br><b>
  <i>“Look at me, Nell,” he commands, softly but firmly. I do. His eyes are hooded and serious. “Turning point, right here. You don’t want this, you have to tell me now. Get up and go. This’ll all be forgotten. I’ll be your friend. But say so now. ‘Cause any further, we’re in it all the way.”<br><br>***<br><br>“How do you compete with a ghost, Colton?” I whisper the question into a long silence. <br>He shrugs. “I don’t know. You don’t. You just understand that there’s a part of you that you can’t give away, because it belongs to a dead person. I don’t know.” <br>“Can we do this? You and me? You with your ghost of India, me with mine of Kyle?” <br>He takes my hands, rubs my knuckles with his thumbs. “All we can do is try, do our best. Give as much as we have to give, one day at a time. One breath at a time... If we want to live, to not be half-ghosts ourselves, stuck loving the memory of someone who’s gone, then we have to try. We understand each other, Nelly. We’ve both lost someone we love. We both have scars and regrets and anger. We can do this together.”<br><br>***<br><br>“I’m not just falling in love with you, Nell. I’m falling into you. You’re an ocean, and I’m falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are. Like you said, it’s scary in a way, but it’s also the most amazing thing I’ve ever experienced. You are the most amazing thing I’ve ever experienced.”<br><br>***<br><br>There’s no magical healing in this. I won’t wake up tomorrow fixed and joyful. I’ll still hurt and grieve. But moments like this, with Colton? They make it all bearable. He doesn’t fix me, doesn’t heal me. He just makes life worthwhile.</i>
</b><br><br>The book is told by dual point of view, both by Nell and Colton. Kyle is never the story teller. The book is emotional, scorching hot and at times, painful. There is death, murder and attempt of rape.<br><br> <img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1485334164ra/21804313.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>And the songs... oh the songs Colton sang added so much beauty to the book.<br><br><b>
  <i>You’re not alone. <br>You are loved. <br>You are held. <br>Quiet your crying voice, lost child. <br>You’re okay, now. You’re okay, now. <br><br>Just hold on, one more day. <br>Just hold on, one more hour. <br>Someone will come for you. <br>Someone will hold you close. <br><br>I know, I know. It’s not okay,<br>It’s not alright. <br>But if you just hold on, <br>One more day, one more hour. <br>It will be. <br>It will be.</i>
</b><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="12598924626330959976" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_562239117" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/562239117" />
    <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog"><img alt="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1416791332p2/4597644.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/562239117?book_show_action=true">Mar 15, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog" href="/user/show/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog">Tessamari ♥Many Waters...♥ ~ Sweet Spot Book Blog</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=explicit">explicit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=hot-and-heavy">hot-and-heavy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=new-adult-mature-ya">new-adult-mature-ya</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=must-re-read-again">must-re-read-again</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=crack-books">crack-books</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=2013">2013</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=first-love-crush">first-love-crush</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy">lead-character-tattooed-and-sexy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4597644-tessamari-many-waters-sweet-spot-book-blog?shelf=ultimate-book-boyfriend">ultimate-book-boyfriend</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer562239117" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9399615271583469611">4.75 Stars<br/><br/><b>
  <i>Fermented grief is far more potent. </i>
</b><br/><br/>HOLY SHIT! Man, this was just what I needed. I was so emotionally invested in Nell’s story, that I could not put this down and easily read this in one sitting. It’s emotional stories like this that make reading so much fun. Fuck. I was a blubbering mess by a third of the way through. It’s not really spoiler<i>-ish</i> considering you know someone important is going to die. I knew I was going to be a hot mess, but waiting for the axe to fall was excrucia</span>
  <span id="freeText9399615271583469611" style="display:none">4.75 Stars<br><br><b>
  <i>Fermented grief is far more potent. </i>
</b><br><br>HOLY SHIT! Man, this was just what I needed. I was so emotionally invested in Nell’s story, that I could not put this down and easily read this in one sitting. It’s emotional stories like this that make reading so much fun. Fuck. I was a blubbering mess by a third of the way through. It’s not really spoiler<i>-ish</i> considering you know someone important is going to die. I knew I was going to be a hot mess, but waiting for the axe to fall was excruciating. Be warned: You will cry. I did. Seriously. How can you move on from a loss like that?<br><br>This was such a unique story simply because I fell in love with the first Hero, Kyle, only to have him taken away <i>like that</i>…well, it broke my heart into a million pieces, I’ll tell you that much. Our main Hero, Colton, had a lot to live up to. How can you replace such a character as Kyle? Just like Nell, I found myself reluctantly drawn to Colton. In a way, it felt <i>wrong</i> to move on, but you honest to God, couldn't help it. I was so torn. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I find myself forgetting him. I see him dying over and over, but I can’t remember what he smelled like. What his arms felt like holding me. What sex with him felt like. What kissing him felt like. I can’t remember him. I can’t remember him. And I wonder sometimes if I ever really loved him. If it was just teenage infatuation. Thinking I loved him because he was my first. Because we’d fucked. I don’t know. I don’t remember. And now there’s you, and you’re…better than he was. Stronger. You turn me on in a way I don’t remember with him. You make me feel things he never did. The way you kiss me, it’s better than I remember his kisses being. When you made me come, I realized I’d never felt anything like it, ever. <u>Ever.</u>”</i>
</b><br><br><u>Nell &amp; Kyle</u><br>After the first few pages of the book, I was HOOKED on Kyle. He was so sweet and so sexy. He and Nell have been best friends since, like, forever. They’re the same age, born only two days apart. Together they learned to ride bikes, did homework, studied and just grew up together. They were thick as thieves and it was assumed that sooner or later they would end up together. Of course both were reluctant to try anything more until one day another boy asked Nell out, and Kyle flipped. Something was about to change between them, and let me tell you, their first kiss: So sweet and so amazing. As in the <i>other</i> firsts they will inevitably have: Exciting, thrilling and HOT. I loved where these two were headed. However, you knew something awful was coming and waiting for that axe to fall was torturous. And when it did fall, I was a just as heartbroken as Nell. It was a horrible feeling. No wonder Nell ended up a fucked up mess. Could she ever get over first love? Could I? <br><br><b>
  <i>But Colton is…I’m safe with him. He draws the truth out of me. He draws the pain out of me. Colton knows pain. He’s intimately familiar with it. Lives with it. Guilt, too.</i>
</b><br><br><u>Nell &amp; Colton</u><br>After falling hard for Kyle, part of me wondered how this author was going to proceed in making me fall for Colton. He had HUGE shoes to fill. Amazingly enough, I slowly fell for him. He left his home at only eighteen, moving to New York. Colton didn’t really become a prevalent character until the day of Kyle’s funeral. Nell and he were practically strangers, but for some reason, while mourning Kyle, they found a small sense of solace with each other, even sharing an illicit kiss. It wasn’t until two years later that fate intervened once more and threw Colton and Nell back together. <br><br><b>
  <i>“I’m not just falling in love with you, Nell. I’m falling into you. You’re an ocean, and I’m falling in, drowning in the depths of who you are. Like you said, it’s scary in a way, but it’s also the most amazing thing I’ve ever experienced. <u>You</u> are the most amazing thing I’ve ever experienced.”</i>
</b> <br><br><i>Le Sigh.</i> They’re both damaged. Nell has never fully healed from losing Kyle. As for Colton, well, we find out there’s a reason for why Colton left home at eighteen, broke and alone in the big city of New York. His story was far more than I expected. He suffered so much since moving out. He is such an amazing character and I can easily say that he is one of those unforgettable Heroes: Beautiful, protective, possessive, and oh so sweet. I Love Colton. All my doubts about loving him as much as Kyle, were shattered once I got to truly know him. <br><br><b>
  <i>“God, fuck me. Don’t <u>do</u> that,” he says, his voice ragged.<br>I’m puzzled. “Do what?”<br>“Bite your lip. It drives me wild. Bite your lip, and it’s over. Your mouth is mine.”</i>
</b><br><br>Fuck! I have no words to describe the intensity of the relationship between Nell and Colton. For me, these two were like each other’s therapy; soothing each other’s wounds to the point where they could finally move on from their past. The way these two communicated, whether it’s through music, or through sex, one thing is for certain: They are fucking <b>intense.</b> The whole story was intense. I just fucking LOVED. Every. Single. Moment. <br><br>-----<br><b>
  <u>FOLLOW ME</u>
</b><br><a href="http://s1094.photobucket.com/user/thessamari/media/Banner2_zps7a6c719e.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_548049137" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/548049137" />
    <a title="Kim Person" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/7590856-kim-person"><img alt="Kim Person" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1434694589p2/7590856.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/548049137?book_show_action=true">Feb 27, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Kim Person" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Kim Person" href="/user/show/7590856-kim-person">Kim Person</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/7590856-kim-person?shelf=arc">arc</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer548049137" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer16237438135601086083">BEYOND 5 stars I mean WAY WAY WAY beyond!! So beautifully written and so emotionally powerful it will leave you thinking of it for days, yes I mean DAYS, after you finish reading it. When Jasinda offered an ARC of Falling Into You ~ in typical Kim fashion I was so.................<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808095.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>The story begins we are introduced to Nell and her BFF, Kyle, they literally have known one another since birth. They have shared everything together and eventually Nell learns that Kyle's feelings for her are more than</span>
  <span id="freeText16237438135601086083" style="display:none">BEYOND 5 stars I mean WAY WAY WAY beyond!! So beautifully written and so emotionally powerful it will leave you thinking of it for days, yes I mean DAYS, after you finish reading it. When Jasinda offered an ARC of Falling Into You ~ in typical Kim fashion I was so.................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808095.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The story begins we are introduced to Nell and her BFF, Kyle, they literally have known one another since birth. They have shared everything together and eventually Nell learns that Kyle's feelings for her are more than friendly when she share's her excitement of being asked on her first date by Kyle's best buddy. At sixteen years of age she was finally able to go out on a "real" date and she was brimming with excitement in typical teenage fashion she was..................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808096.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>We watch Kyle &amp; Nell's relationship evolves and deepens. They are each other's forever, one true love, and ultimate soul mate. We experience their first.........................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808097.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and each of theirs first with one another .......................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380403990ra/786043.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Fast forward to age 18 and they've graduated from High School and they each have respective colleges they are looking forward to going to but their parents have agreed they can go up to Kyle's parents cabin together and all alone. They are beyond excited to get away and spend time together. This part of the book totally endeared to me to Kyle and his love for Nell ~ oh, how he loved her with everything he had in him. What's supposed to be the most memory turns into ~ the most heartrending scene I've read in a book in such a very long time. It was at this part I completely.......................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380410439ra/804701.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>The shock, pain, and absolute gut wrenching point of the book brought me to my knees. It was everything I didn't want to happen. It was tragic and so very sad but so poignantly written I felt that what I read truly happened ~ that I was there when it happened as I listened to Kyle repeatedly tell Nell he loved her. The selfish act he performed further provide just how much he loved her. Poor sweet Nell, the depth of her sorrow and guilt ~ oh the guilt ~ placing the blame on herself will make you want to grab her and....................................<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411446i/808098.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>She's literally a shell of the person she once was and she comes face to face with Kyle's older brother Colton. The proverbial "black sheep" of the family. Nell doesn't know why but she feels an instant connection to him one she certainly doesn't feel is appropriate and again the guilt she feels at that is right there on the pages that you feel what she's feeling. Colton's piercing blue eyes, his captivating voice and his guitar playing would've had me on my knees worshipping him immediately ~ well perhaps not so immediate but I certainly wouldn't of been able to look him in the eyes without getting lost. <br><br>The book fast forwards and the story switches to Colton's POV. This was brilliant on Jasinda's part ~ He's in NYC busking just sitting there............................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/506693.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>when who does he see standing behind the small crowd that gathered? well none other than Nell herself. She's captivating, beautiful and holding a guitar case. She joins him and they play together and when she starts singing he's blown away by this angel's voice. He also sees that she hasn't moved on without Kyle. The pain is there in her eyes and he knows he shouldn't get involved but again that magnetic connection they have draws him to her. He wants to spend time with her, but doesn't think he is good enough for her. <br><br>Now ladies I have to tell you from this point on I will walk you through the remainder of this beautiful book with the emotions I felt. Colton saves Nell from the Neanderthal he saw her with when she walked into his good friends bar where he was playing. Yes he totally.......<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808099.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Not wanting to be alone he takes her back to his place and things get.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1380411446i/808100.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>but both Colton &amp; Nelly-baby (his sweet name for her) have ghosts to contend with and not just the most obvious one, Kyle. No Colton opens up to Nell. He describes how he left home immediately after barely graduating high school~ he jumped a bus to NYC with no money, barely any food and he did what he had to do to survive on the streets. Colton came from an affluent family and he learned first hand how to survive all alone, no money, no food, no family, and no friends until he was taken into his "new family." What Colton did to survive and what he ultimately lost again made me thinking .................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808101.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was beginning to think I needed to buy stock in Kleenex because this book had me in tears more time than not. Oh sure there were times I <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808102.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>and then when the sexy Colton shows his dominant side in the "bedroom" and him and Nell finally finish was briefly started. Well HOT STEAMY SEXY throw me down and have your way with me is an understatement. Ladies this was......................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808103.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>it was off the charts but I really didn't expect anything less given the chemistry between the two. Oh yes those two had chemistry BIG TIME and the way Jasinda wrote the sex scenes had me fanning myself. Heck if it wasn't 3 a.m. my hubby wouldn't have been.....................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808104.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I watched their relationship develop. I watched the first time they performed on stage together ~ they were a huge hit. I watched their day to day interactions and I wasn't even close to being done and I thought man can this get any better? I also had a little feeling that this was going to ....................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808105.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>The story had switched back to Nell's POV before then and when she find something out she did the last thing I thought she would do................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808106.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I read that part and ......................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808107.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>but Colton his a take charge kind of guy and there was no way he was going to let her go and he does the first thing I expected him to do! He hopped on a .....................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808108.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>straight to her folks house! Barging in demanding to know where Nell was and when he found her well darn it I was........................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380369063ra/721740.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was so ...........................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/354491.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>No, No, No I thought as I flicked through the pages on my Kindle. Please NO ~ Why of Why and when Colton drops a little bomb about his past I was .........................................................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808109.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>How much more grief can two people suffer? Well, Colton &amp; Nell proved that they did have the strength to pick up the pieces and move forward. By the end of this book I was...............................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380222758ra/506419.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>I was so happy ~ no two people out there have ever deserved the ending that got!!! Jasinda this book was pure ............................<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380411446ra/808110.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>you Jasinda! Falling Into You was a deeply emotional read for me. It touched me in ways that I never thought it would for a fiction read! I'm not kidding I was so engrossed in the story that I lost myself in it and I did have to remind myself that I was not part of the story, but isn't that what makes up some of the most amazing reads? A story that draws you in and you have no clue how deeply you will be drawn into it until you finish and you look around and realize no that didn't just happen to you but it sure the heck felt like it did. A story where I lost track of time and that I was so sad to see it had ended. <br><br>You will not be able to put this one down. To even give it a rating of 5 stars would be an insult this book FAR exceeds 5 stars! This has become my TOP read of 2013~ yes it topped the most recent release that everyone had been waiting ages for to come out. If Goodreads could allow me to add another 5 stars at the top it's easily 10 stars for me. It had EVERYTHING I want out of a book ~ first love, sheer gut wrenching heartbreak, angst, forgiveness in different forms, over the top oh I would love to have some of that in between the sheet scenes, smiles, laughter and most of all a chance for two people getting a second chance at love and perhaps just perhaps finding their true soul mate regardless what they may had thought before.<br><br>This is a book that should clearly be put at your TBR list now ~ No wait this is a book that you need to BUY NOW, START NOW, and forget whatever the outside "real" world demands of you and read it. I promise you won't be able to put this one down. I promise it's so brilliantly and beautifully written and in such a way that you will forget your reading a book ~ you will be reading the stories of two broken, damaged people finding the strength to believe in and let themselves love again. <br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16237438135601086083" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('vEAx3/q33saYq1brqJzYO62AowzsKOWeDHnpMFEV876GZlgNQekXrj+A4opfadLke99ExCKla/lXB6+BnFYBJA==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('Se2snpEu4ppabSSbdCLuFamqNDqxnDSGZaFz5AjnwUFzy8VMKnAr8v1GkPqD1+TKf/XT8n8RuuE+3zVVxaQz2w==')})
  }
//]]>

Quiet and reserved, Callie still fears letting anyone else into her world. But Kayden is certain that Callie has come back into his life for a reason.   <span id="freeText2926157391682129685" style="display:none">NEW YORK TIMES, USA TODAY, WALL STREET JOURNAL and international bestselling author Jasinda Wilder is a Michigan native with a penchant for titillating tales about sexy men and strong women.       });

      newTip['wrapper'].addClassName('prototipAllowOverflow');

        $('bookCover_22812308').observe('prototip:shown', function () {
